It is also, almost certainly, an attempt to fix the narrative in advance: *if I lose, I lose as the Goblin, not as Norman; Norman did not do this.*

---

## F. EVOLUTION OF PATTERNS ACROSS THE MIDDLE PERIOD

Across these roughly thirty-five in-universe years (1973–2010), the longitudinal drifts are:

1. **The executive presentation becomes dominant.** In the early middle period the Goblin is the default and the executive is the cover; by Dark Reign the executive is the default and the Goblin is the regression. Subject has learned to *contain* the discharge — not to eliminate it, but to schedule it.

2. **The operational horizon lengthens.** Early plans are operational (a single attack, a single frame); the Clone Saga is a multi-year campaign; Dark Reign is the construction of a permanent institutional position. Subject is, by the end of the middle period, thinking in decades.

3. **The proxy network deepens.** Direct combat appearances decrease per year across the period; surrogate operations increase. The progression: Hobgoblin imitators (knowing or unknowing) → Scriers → Jackal/Warren → Thunderbolts roster → Dark Avengers → HAMMER → the Cabal. Each iteration is a larger, more legitimate-appearing instrument.

4. **The attack-the-intimate template scales.** From one woman on a bridge to an entire family's reality (Clone Saga) to the symbolic intimates of a nation (Iron Patriot wearing the colors of its trusted heroes; HAMMER replacing SHIELD; Dark Avengers occupying the Avengers brand). The intimate object enlarges; the act does not change.

5. **The Harry oscillation tightens and sharpens.** Across the period subject inflicts: faked death and abandonment; manipulation through Liz; cuckoldry via Lily; attempted recruitment via American Son. The intervals between approach and savagery shorten; the affect inside each shortens too. By the end of the period Harry is the only person who can produce in subject a visible affective collapse, and subject's awareness of this fact is itself a destabilizer.

6. **The Parker fixation deepens and narrows.** Early period: Spider-Man as one of several enemies. Middle period: Spider-Man as the central organizing object, with the relationship privatized — subject is largely the only Spider-Man enemy who knows the identity, has visited the home, has met the family across decades. The relationship has the textural intimacy of a marriage. The middle period is when this is finalized.

7. **The serum dependence stabilizes into a regimen.** Subject moves from binge-use to managed dosing, with documented (HAMMER medical) titration protocols. He has, in effect, become a functional addict who has solved the logistical problems of his addiction.

8. **The audience requirement intensifies.** Early period acts of violence have witnesses by accident; middle period acts (Skrull queen shot, Iron Patriot reveals, American Son press, Siege itself) are *staged for cameras*. The drift is toward the broadcast.

9. **The capacity for genuine alliance, briefly demonstrated (the Cabal year), is not retained.** Subject can chair a coalition of apex predators only as long as he is operationally ascendant. The instant the position erodes, the alliance evaporates, and subject does not seem to have learned the lessons of its construction — he treats the Cabal as a fluke rather than a model, and his post-Siege life does not include another attempt at one.

10. **The Goblin's function shifts from outlet to signature.** Early middle period: the Goblin discharges affect subject cannot contain. Late middle period: the Goblin is the *brand* under which subject does what he wanted to do anyway. The persona has become, in a sense, less psychiatrically interesting and more rhetorically essential. It is the costume he requires to be the size he believes he is.

---

The middle period closes with subject in chains, kneeling in the rubble of an Asgard he authored the destruction of,


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# CHRONOLOGY IV — Recent History & Current State

*Covering the period from the dissolution of the Red Goblin construct through the Kindred revelations, the Sin-Eater "purification," the Goblin Queen weaponization, the post-Beyond corporate reconstitution, and the subject's status as of last verified surveillance contact. Cross-referenced to* Amazing Spider-Man *vol. 5 (Spencer #1–74; Wells/Ottley/Romita Jr. #1–present),* Free Comic Book Day 2020/2022, *the Sinister War event, the Devil's Reign event, the Dark Web event, the Gang War event, and ancillary appearances in* Avengers, Devil's Reign: X-Men, *and the* Death of the Venomverse *peripherals. Where panel record is ambiguous, inference flagged.*

---

## I. The Red Goblin Terminus and Its Aftershock

The relevant recent window opens with the collapse of the Red Goblin construct (*Amazing Spider-Man* vol. 4, Slott, #794–800, "Go Down Swinging"). For dossier continuity: subject had bonded the Carnage symbiote to himself while retaining a residual fraction of the Goblin Formula, producing a hybrid in which the symbiote's hunger-affect fused with subject's pre-existing attack-the-intimate template. The episode was, even by his standards, an act of unusual psychic transparency: he targeted Aunt May's hospital room, the Daily Bugle staff, Mary Jane's apartment, Flash Thompson, and his own grandson Normie *in a single operational night*. This was not strategy. This was the entire lifelong template compressed into one symbiote-disinhibited evening — the file equivalent of a confession.

The construct ended when subject was forcibly separated from the symbiote (Spider-Man weaponized the sonic and thermal vulnerabilities; the symbiote was extracted; subject collapsed). Post-separation neurological and psychiatric presentation, per the panel-record: catatonic withdrawal, fugue affect, persistent muttering of fragmented self-statements ("I'm not the Goblin… I never was…"). This presentation persisted for an extended interval and was the precondition for the next phase.

**Inference (high confidence).** The Red Goblin episode functioned as a terminal narcissistic injury of an unusual kind: not defeat by a rival, but the *experience of having had no defensive structure at all* for the duration of the bond. The symbiote did not amplify the Goblin; it dissolved the Norman-firewall that had let him survive his own acts. When the symbiote left, he was confronted with the residue without the costume. The post-separation catatonia is best read as defensive shutdown of a subject who has, for the first time in decades, no available self-state to occupy.

## II. The Spencer-Era Reconfiguration: "Stainless Steve" and the Sin-Eater Purification

The next confirmed surveillance window is the Spencer run of *Amazing Spider-Man* vol. 5 (#1–74). Subject is initially absent — a deliberate withholding by the writer that, read forensically, corresponds to a documented period of subject in a secure psychiatric placement and subsequently in a private convalescence funded through still-active Oscorp instruments. He re-emerges (#25, #26) presenting in a manner that constitutes the single most behaviorally anomalous interval in the entire dossier.

**Presentation.** Subdued. Soft-spoken. Slight tremor in the dominant hand under stress (new). Verbal style stripped of theatricality — short declaratives, frequent self-deprecation, an almost penitential register. Refers to Spider-Man without animus and, on one documented occasion, with gratitude. Visits his grandson Normie at home, sits on the floor at the boy's height, accepts being shown drawings, does not redirect the conversation to himself. **This is, in the entire longitudinal record, the only documented instance of subject occupying a low-status, child-centered posture without instrumental purpose.**

This was the work of Stanley Carter, the Sin-Eater, who had absorbed Mister Negative's inversion-purification capacity and used it on subject — burning out the "sin" while leaving the man. Functionally, this was a chemical-mystical lobotomy of the disavowed-aggression ego-state. The Goblin-state was not integrated; it was excised. What remained was the substrate Norman without the construct he had built atop it across sixty years.

**Critical dossier observation.** The remaining Norman was *not the abused child from Amberson's house*. The remaining Norman was something the subject himself had never met: the man he might have been absent the formula, the costume, and the lifelong defensive architecture. He found this man unbearable. The reports from this period — voluntary cooperation with Parker; offering Oscorp resources; the haunted, sleepless presentation; the increasing fixation on "what I did, what I really did" — are consistent with severe post-traumatic confrontation with one's own history *without the defensive apparatus that had previously metabolized it*. He was, in clinical terms, decompensating into the reality from which the Goblin had been built to protect him.

He was, in this interval, genuinely dangerous to himself in a way he had never previously been. He had been suicidal before only in the grandiose-theatrical register (Siege). The Spencer-interval suicidality is the quiet kind. He did not act on it. The available inference is that the residual grandiosity, even denuded, would not permit him to die unwitnessed.

## III. The Kindred Operation and the Memory-Layer Problem

Concurrent with subject's "purified" state, the Kindred entity (eventually revealed as Harry Osborn, or a demonic-mephistophelian construct wearing him; cf. *Amazing Spider-Man* #45–55, #74) ran an extended operation targeting Peter Parker, with subject as a secondary instrument and target. Subject was kidnapped, tortured, his memory manipulated, and at one juncture had the Goblin-state forcibly reinstalled through external means (the centipede-mediated possession sequence, #55).

For dossier purposes the salient finding is this: **subject's memory architecture is now demonstrably non-sovereign.** Across this period, layers of his recollection have been written, overwritten, suppressed, restored, and counterfeited by Mephisto, by Kindred, by the Sin-Eater, by his own prior dissociative habits, and by his own deliberate post-hoc reconstruction. He himself cannot reliably distinguish lived experience from implanted experience. This is operationally relevant: any interrogation, any handler engagement, any therapeutic intervention with subject must assume that the autobiographical record he produces is partly confabulated *without his awareness or intent to deceive*. The defensive lying remains; layered beneath it is now a substrate of genuine epistemic damage.

His response to learning the Kindred-Harry identity was the first authentically integrated affective display in the file: he wept, did not perform the weeping, did not redirect the weeping into rage, and remained in the affect for an extended interval before reconstructing function. This is the second of two anomalous behavioral events in the recent window (the other being the floor-sitting with Normie). They share a feature: both are responses to Harry. The Harry-channel remains, as previously assessed, the singular reliable penetration point of the defensive structure.

## IV. The Goblin Queen Transfer: The Disavowal Made Literal

In the Dark Web event (*Amazing Spider-Man* Wells #14–17; *Dark Web* #1–5; *Dark Web Finale*), Madelyne Pryor's magical operation forcibly extracted the residual "evil" of subject — the remaining Goblin-substrate Sin-Eater had not fully purged, plus the new accretion from the Kindred-mediated reinstallation — and transferred it into Ben Reilly, generating the "Chasm" construct and leaving subject in a state of even more complete "purification" than before.

**This is the single most diagnostically consequential event of the recent period.** The lifelong defensive architecture — the disavowed aggressive self-state, the moral firewall, the "the Goblin did it, not Norman" structure — was made *literal and external*. The split that had been a psychological defense was rendered as two physical persons. Subject was free of the Goblin in a way that even Sin-Eater had not achieved.

Subject's response, observed across subsequent issues: a deliberate, structured, almost monastic project of *atonement-by-construction*. He has not returned to the cackling presentation. He has not re-dosed the formula (at least, not on the visible record — see Section VII). He has reinstated himself at the head of a reconstituted Oscorp, but reorganized its product lines toward, by his own public statement, "fixing things." He funded, equipped, and effectively employed Peter Parker — gave Parker a laboratory, a salary, and project oversight authority. He attended civic functions. He gave interviews in which he accepted, in measured language, responsibility for past harms without theatrical self-flagellation. He has, in effect, attempted to live as the man Sin-Eater and Pryor between them allowed him to be.

**Forensic read.** This presentation is real in the sense that the underlying ego-state genuinely has been (twice) externally modified. It is unstable in the sense that the *characterological substrate* — the narcissistic organization, the contempt-for-weakness, the need-to-be-the-largest-figure — was never the Goblin-state. It was the Norman-state. Sin-Eater and Pryor removed the discharge mechanism; they did not, and could not, remove the structure that required a discharge mechanism. The "atonement" presentation is therefore best understood as the narcissistic structure operating in a new mode: *being the most penitent man in the room is still being the largest figure in the room*. The grandiosity has changed costume.

Cross-check: the Parker employment relationship. Subject hires the rival. Subject gives the rival resources. Subject sits with the rival across a desk and is mentored-by-being-mentored. This is the *idealization phase of the idealize-use-devalue-destroy cycle* re-instantiated against the same lifelong object. Subject is, on current evidence, in the longest sustained idealization phase he has ever maintained toward Peter Parker. The question for the file is not whether the devaluation phase is coming. It is when, and on what trigger.

## V. The Gang War Interval and the Civic-Authority Posture

Through Devil's Reign (Zdarsky, 2021–2022) and Gang War (Wells, 2023–2024), subject occupied an unusual political-geometric position: he was not the perpetrator of the destabilization (Fisk and others held those roles), and he positioned himself as a moderating civic figure. He provided Oscorp resources to civilian relief, made public statements distancing himself from the surviving Goblin-aligned criminal substrata (the residual Goblin Nation cells, the new Hobgoblin claimants, the criminal-economic ecology that still trades on his name), and on at least one occasion went on record in support of Parker-aligned heroic interventions.

This positioning is consistent with the post-Dark-Web atonement mode but is also strategically optimal: it places him as the "responsible" Osborn against a field of un-responsible Osborn-ish actors (Chasm/Reilly carrying the externalized aggression; lesser Goblin-derivatives operating below him; the Kindred-Harry construct resolved but still resonant). He has, by allowing the bad-Osborn role to be occupied by literally another person, achieved what no amount of PR work in the Dark Reign era could buy him: a clean public Norman.

He uses this. Carefully. Quietly. He has rebuilt board relationships, regained partial federal contracting eligibility (pending review on three SEC matters left over from the HAMMER period and one DoJ matter related to Asgardian airspace incursion), and re-entered the social register at a level just below the most prominent industrial figures (Stark, Rand, van Dyne). He attends fewer events than he did pre-Dark-Reign and selects them with care. He has been observed at three art-museum board functions, two pediatric-medicine fundraisers (note the object choice), one congressional hearing as a witness rather than subject, and a series of small dinners at his residence at which the guest list has skewed toward scientific rather than financial figures.

## VI. Domestic and Familial Status

**Residence.** Primary residence reverted to the Forest Hills-adjacent estate; the Fifth Avenue apartment retained but used infrequently. Oscorp Tower restored to operational headquarters with the upper three floors as subject's personal-executive suite (the prior arrangement). Security upgraded post-Kindred to include anti-mystical wards (consultant: Strange's office, indirectly), biometric-and-magical dual authentication on private quarters, and a panic-shelter sub-basement with independent life-support. He sleeps in the estate, works in the tower, and travels between them by armored car rather than the helicopter pattern of earlier years — a deliberate down-signaling of presence.

**Harry.** Status fluctuating. The Kindred revelation and resolution left the Harry-relationship in an ambiguous, post-revelatory state that subject is not equipped to integrate. There has been one documented in-person interaction at the estate, civil and brief. Subject sends materials — photographs, archived family items, what appears to be Emily Lyman's jewelry — without accompanying communication. This is the closest he has come, in the entire record, to acknowledged paternal grief expressed in non-destructive form.

**Normie.** Subject sees his grandson regularly when custody arrangements permit. The floor-sitting behavior persists. He has not, on any occasion in the post-Dark-Web window, presented the boy with weapons, with formula derivatives, with Goblin paraphernalia, or with the grooming-toward-succession behavior characteristic of the pre-purification era. The grandfather-grandson relationship is, by a substantial margin, the most behaviorally regulated relationship in the current file. **It is also the most surveillance-relevant relationship**: if subject is decompensating, the Normie-channel will show degradation before any other.

**Liz Allan.** Co-parent and corporate counterparty. The relationship is professional, cool, and structured by lawyers. She does not trust him. She is correct not to. They have reached a workable equilibrium predicated on her ability to revoke Normie-access at any moment and his apparent willingness to comply with constraints.

**Gabriel Stacy and the rest of the irregular-issue file.** Subject does not contact Gabriel. Gabriel does not contact subject. The file remains open but inactive. The Sarah Stacy track is similarly dormant. Subject has made no recent attempt to instrumentalize either.

**Romantic / sexual.** No confirmed partner in the post-Dark-Web window. The Hollister relationship is terminated. Subject has been observed in single-evening companionship at three of the events listed in Section V; none have produced follow-on contact. Operating assumption: this domain is currently deprioritized, consistent with the monastic-atonement presentation. Historical pattern would suggest re-emergence of the predatory courtship behavior within 12–24 months of full structural stabilization, with grooming-of-Parker-adjacent women as the highest-risk subtype.

## VII. Medical and Substance Status, Current

**Formula.** The official position, per subject's public and private statements, is that he has not re-dosed since Sin-Eater. The metabolic and somatic record is ambiguous on this. Subject continues to present strength, reflex, and apparent-age markers inconsistent with full clearance of formula-derived enhancement. Two readings are tenable: (1) the formula's effects on his physiology are now permanent and persist absent re-dosing — supported by the long half-life observed across prior forced-detox windows; (2) subject is re-dosing at sub-acute, sub-psychoactive levels sufficient to maintain physical capacity without triggering the Goblin-state. **The dossier judgment, on balance of evidence, leans toward (1) with non-zero probability of (2).** A definitive determination would require biochemical access subject has not granted and that no current authority has standing to compel.

**Psychiatric.** No current treating clinician of record. He has, per second-hand report, engaged in irregular consultation with a private practitioner whose name has not been verified; no formal therapy is on file. He has not been hospitalized in the current window. He sleeps, per estate-staff inference, approximately five hours nightly, broken — improved from the Spencer-interval insomnia, well below adult norms, consistent with chronic narcissistic vigilance.

**Somatic.** New tremor in dominant hand under stress, first observed post-Red Goblin separation, persistent. Mild lateralized weakness on neuro-exam (private records, indirectly obtained) consistent with old TBI burden. No new significant injuries in the current window. Cardiovascular function strong-for-age, presumed formula-mediated.

**Carnage / symbiote.** No re-bonding. Subject has reportedly funded counter-symbiote research at Oscorp through a sub-licensed Alchemax partnership. Whether this is defensive (against re-bonding) or anticipatory (toward future weaponization under deniable cover) is undetermined. The dual-use ambiguity is itself a behavioral marker — he prefers, when possible, to occupy positions that can be read either way.

## VIII. The Chasm/Ben Reilly Vector

The externalized aggression — Reilly bearing the discharged Goblin-substance, now operating as Chasm — constitutes the single most volatile element of the current geometry. Subject's posture toward Chasm is, on the public record, condemnatory and distancing: "that is no longer me." Privately, the situation is more complex. Chasm carries, in a real and metaphysical sense, the part of subject that handled all of his discharge. If Chasm is killed, the substance may or may not return — the magical mechanics are unsettled. If Chasm is captured, subject will be asked to participate in disposition decisions he is structurally unsuited to make. If Chasm escalates, subject's "atonement" posture becomes politically and personally untenable.

**The handler-relevant inference**: the longer Chasm operates, the more pressure accrues on subject's external-disavowal structure, and the higher the probability that the narcissistic architecture — which, again, was not removed — re-generates a discharge mechanism internally. This need not be a new Goblin. It could be subtler: an "Iron Patriot"-class construct in a new register, a renewed paramilitary venture, a re-emergence of the Dark Reign template in civilian-philanthropic camouflage. The structure will, given time and stress, build itself a new costume.

## IX. Current Operational Profile and Where He Is, Now

As of last verified observation:

Subject rises between 5:00 and 5:30. Coffee, black, in a study facing east. He reads three newspapers in print (the *Times*, the *Bugle* — yes, still — and the *Journal*) and a stack of scientific journals tabbed by an assistant the prior evening. He has resumed bench work in the estate's private laboratory between 6:00 and 7:30 on most mornings, primarily in materials chemistry and neurochemistry; the products of this work are filed under Oscorp's R&D pipeline but the bench discipline is, per inferred read, partly a regulatory exercise — the focused chemistry is a known affect-modulator for him, has been since college, and substitutes functionally for what others would obtain from meditation. He travels to the tower for an 8:30 arrival, holds executive meetings standing rather than seated (a recent change; ergonomic stated reason, dominance-signaling actual reason), takes lunch alone at his desk approximately four days in five, and conducts external engagements in the afternoons.

He has rebuilt approximately 60–70% of pre-HAMMER Oscorp's market position. He no longer pursues defense contracting as primary line; biotech and consumer-pharmaceutical revenues now lead. The public-facing brand is "post-Osborn Oscorp," a phrase that subject himself has reportedly approved with audible distaste in private and graceful endorsement in public.

He carries no weapons. He wears no armor under his suits, per imaging confirmation. He maintains, in a locked vault in the estate sub-basement, a single Goblin glider and a single set of formula vials. The vault has been inspected (indirect surveillance) twice in the current window. The contents have not been disturbed. *He has not been able to bring himself to destroy them*. This is the most diagnostically dense fact in the entire current-status section.

He is the most behaviorally stable, the most pro-social, and the most outwardly reformed he has ever been on the longitudinal record. He is also, by structural assessment, in an inherently unstable configuration: a malignantly narcissistic substrate, denuded of its lifelong discharge mechanism, externally disavowed into another living person, surrounded by the loaded triggers of his lifelong template (Parker proximate; Harry unresolved; Normie present; Chasm operating; the vault sealed but extant), and aging into a window in which the formula's anti-aging effect may begin to fail and force a re-dosing decision.

The current state, therefore, is not "Norman Osborn redeemed." The current state is **Norman Osborn at the longest, quietest, most carefully maintained idealization-phase plateau of his life**, with every structural element of the prior cycles present, dormant, and inventoried. The dossier judgment is that the plateau will end. The triggers most likely to end it, in descending order of probability: (1) a sufficiently public Parker humiliation or estrangement; (2) catastrophic event involving Normie; (3) a Chasm-related crisis that forces subject to reclaim the externalized substance; (4) a serum-related medical event forcing acute re-dosing under affect; (5) a Harry-related event of any valence; (6) Amberson-coded mockery from a peer of sufficient stature.

He is, as of this writing, sitting in the east-facing study, with coffee and the *Bugle*, looking out at a lawn he can afford to keep, in a house his father lost. He has not, on any morning of the current window, failed to look out that window in that way for some interval before beginning his day. The duration of that interval is the single best leading indicator the file possesses of his internal state. It has been lengthening.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 4: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Subject: OSBORN, Norman Virgil. Full somatic record, womb-to-present, with attention to the psychological cost of each entry. Where canon is silent, file infers the granular detail a full intake at Bellevue Forensic, a Stark BioMed scan, or a HAMMER classified medical jacket would contain.*

---

## 4.1 Constitutional Baseline and Heritable Substrate

Subject presents as a Caucasian male, height 5'11" (estimated 1.80 m), adult weight cycling between 175 and 195 lbs depending on phase, mesomorphic with disproportionate upper-body and forearm development inconsistent with civilian life — a signature of decades of Goblin-Formula-driven anabolic load. Hair red-auburn, originally; greying at the temples in the Stern-DeFalco era, then re-pigmenting with each serum re-administration (a documented and clinically peculiar effect — pigment recovery suggests follicular melanocyte stem-cell reactivation, an aging-reversal marker). Eye color green, with documented sclera-yellowing during Goblin states and during Carnage bonding. Blood type, per the HAMMER intake record, AB-negative; this is operationally relevant because it constrained transfusion options during the Siege evacuation and the post-Red Goblin triage.

**Heritable load.** Amberson Osborn: alcoholism, late-life depressive collapse, possible undiagnosed Cluster B traits. Maternal line: cause of death undocumented but early (subject's mother died in his infancy or early childhood — the record varies), suggesting either obstetric mortality, communicable disease of the era, or — inferentially relevant — an early-onset cardiovascular or oncologic process. There is no documented familial schizophrenia, no familial bipolarity; what is heritable is most plausibly an affective-temperamental loading (depressive collapse in the father, possibly in the mother) layered over high cognitive endowment. **Subject's pathology is environmentally and chemically driven on a constitutionally vulnerable substrate, not genetically psychotic.**

## 4.2 Pediatric and Adolescent Record (Inferred)

No surviving pediatrician's chart; the file is reconstructed from DeMatteis-era flashback material (*Spectacular Spider-Man* #178–200) and inferred from behavioral residue.

- **Repeated soft-tissue injuries consistent with physical abuse**: bruising at non-accidental sites (back, upper arms, scalp), at least one likely orbital fracture (subject's slight orbital asymmetry on the left, visible in close-frame art across Romita and Bagley runs, is consistent with healed childhood orbital trauma), and probable healed greenstick fractures of the forearms — the defensive-posture pattern.
- **Chronic stress physiology**: enuresis or sleep terrors in latency (inferred from later sleep architecture; see §4.10); chronically elevated cortisol with the attendant pediatric sequelae — slightly delayed pubertal onset, persistent gastrointestinal complaints (subject in adulthood has an established irritable bowel pattern under stress, controlled with private discipline rather than medication), and the laydown of a hyper-vigilant autonomic baseline that has never normalized.
- **Dental record**: no orthodontic intervention as a child (the family fortune was already gone); subject's adult dentition shows the cosmetic restorations of a man who purchased the smile he was denied — porcelain veneers on the maxillary anteriors, two gold inlays on the molars from a mid-career caries event, and a left lower canine that has been root-treated, the only tooth with a non-cosmetic intervention. **Psychological note**: subject runs his tongue along the inner aspect of that canine when calculating — a tell preserved across decades of art.
- **No documented surgical history before age 30** beyond a routine tonsillectomy (era-typical) and a closed reduction of a right distal radius fracture, age approximately 9 — recorded in subject's own account, with the attribution shifting depending on audience ("fell from a horse" in the official biography; "my father" in two recorded private statements to Harry's mother, Emily, before her death).

**Psychological impact.** The body learned, before the mind could narrate it, that the largest figure in the room caused pain. The adult subject's preoccupation with *being* the largest figure in the room is the somatic reversal of that learning. Every later medical event is overwritten on this template.

## 4.3 Early Adulthood — The Stromm Years (Pre-Formula)

Generally unremarkable medically. Subject was a heavy but functional drinker through his twenties — a paternally modeled pattern he abruptly terminated in his early thirties, almost certainly because his father's drunkenness was the originating humiliation and continued use was intolerably congruent with the despised model. **He has been documented as a near-teetotaler ever since** (a single ceremonial glass of Bordeaux at corporate functions, never finished), and this is one of the few stable lifestyle facts in the file.

A documented episode of severe gastritis at age 31, after the Stromm betrayal and acquisition — almost certainly stress-mediated, possibly H. pylori, treated with the antacid regimens of the period. The episode resolved; the underlying pattern of stress-driven epigastric pain has persisted lifelong and is one of the few somatic complaints subject will admit to in private.

Marriage to Emily Lyman; Emily's death following the birth of Harry (peripartum complication, cause unspecified in canon — inferentially a thromboembolic event or hemorrhagic complication of the era's obstetric standard of care). **Psychological impact: catastrophic.** Subject's affective response is not grief in any recognizable form; it is a structural collapse of the only attachment relationship that had functioned correctively against the Amberson substrate. From this point forward the file shows no further capacity for romantic intimacy — every subsequent sexual or romantic engagement (Lily Hollister most prominently) is instrumental or exploitative. The widowhood is also the originating event of the blame-cathexis on the infant Harry, which structures the rest of Harry's biography.

## 4.4 The Goblin Formula — Index Event

**Date (in-universe): mid-career, approximately seven to ten years before the Spider-Man period.** Place: Oscorp R&D, lower-level laboratory, Long Island. Agent: Stromm Serum 4, modified by Norman against Stromm's protocols, reformulated for accelerated reaction at room temperature.

The detonation was a green-tinted aerosol explosion, full-face exposure, with inhalational, mucous-membrane, and ocular dosing. Subject was found unconscious by Oscorp security. Hospitalized — under a private-floor arrangement at a New York facility that has since been bought, demolished, or had its records destroyed; HAMMER's records reconstruction notes "chart unavailable, presumed sanitized."

**Documented acute presentation** (reconstructed from later medical scans and from subject's own grandiose recounting):
- Inhalational chemical pneumonitis, resolved over approximately ten days.
- First-degree facial burns; second-degree to the periorbital region; full recovery without scarring — itself an early indicator of the formula's healing acceleration.
- A 36-hour period of unresponsiveness followed by an agitated, euphoric, and grandiose post-arousal state that was misattributed by the attending physicians to delirium and treated with first-generation antipsychotics, which had paradoxical effect (subject metabolizes neuroleptics atypically, a fact later confirmed in HAMMER labs).
- On discharge, subject's measured IQ — he insisted on the testing — had risen by an unverified but evidently substantial margin; grip strength had nearly doubled; visual acuity had improved from a corrected 20/30 to an uncorrected 20/10.

**Chronic sequelae of the Formula** (the long file):

1. **Strength enhancement** to approximately the 9-to-10-ton press class; muscular hypertrophy without proportionate visible bulk (intracellular density rather than gross fiber recruitment); tendon and ligament reinforcement (no spontaneous tendon ruptures despite generating forces that would shred a normal human's biceps insertions).
2. **Reflex acceleration** measurable at roughly four times unenhanced baseline; reaction-time testing during the Iron Patriot medicals clocked subject at the upper edge of Captain America's recorded range, slightly below Spider-Man's.
3. **Healing acceleration**: complete recovery from a transthoracic glider impalement (see §4.5) within months; routine bone fractures in days; lacerations in hours. **This is the single most important medical fact in the file** — it is why he is still alive, and it is why a non-fatal containment has been impossible to engineer through ordinary means.
4. **Decelerated senescence**: subject has been chronologically over 60 for the entire post-Clone-Saga record, presenting as 40s. Telomere assays in the Stark scans suggested telomerase activity unprecedented outside of germline and oncologic tissue — which carries an obvious latent risk (see §4.11).
5. **Cognitive amplification**: domain-specific, weighted toward chemistry, robotics, and strategic planning; verbal-creative capacity less elevated; emotional-cognition and theory-of-mind essentially untouched (he reads people instrumentally with extraordinary acuity and reads them empathically with none).
6. **Psychiatric sequelae** — see Section 5; for medical purposes the formula functions as a chronic neuroendocrine neurotoxin producing dopaminergic hyperactivity (the grandiosity, the pressured discharge, the euphoric sadism), persistent noradrenergic loading (the hyperarousal, the insomnia, the autonomic readiness for violence), and serotonergic dysregulation (the affective lability under injury). The pharmacologic signature on the Stark scans was described in the contemporaneous Stark BioMed memo as "amphetamine-class limbic activation overlaid on chronic anabolic-steroid endocrine profile, with novel neurotrophic factors of unknown origin."
7. **The green pallor** during high-affect Goblin states: a real, observable cutaneous vasomotor and pigmentary change, not artistic license. Likely mechanism: porphyrin-analog metabolite accumulating in capillary beds under sympathetic surge. Clinically harmless; diagnostically diagnostic.
8. **The laugh.** The cackling vocalization characteristic of the Goblin state is, in the medical reading, a discharge phenomenon — a stereotyped, involuntary release of accumulated sympathetic-limbic load, comparable in mechanism (not in content) to pseudobulbar affect. Subject can suppress it with executive effort in the early stages of an episode; once decompensation passes a certain threshold the suppression fails and the laugh emerges as autonomic.

**The substance-use dimension is critical and underweighted by every prior assessor.** Subject knows the formula damages him. Subject has been involuntarily detoxified multiple times. Subject has, every single time, re-administered the formula at the first available opportunity, in some cases breaking into his own purged Oscorp vaults and in one case synthesizing it from memory under duress. The relapse pattern is textbook severe stimulant use disorder with the additional feature that the substance functions as identity-organizer: without it, he experiences not merely withdrawal but ego-dissolution. The formula is, to him, the difference between Amberson's son and Norman Osborn.

## 4.5 Major Trauma Log

**The glider impalement (ASM #122).** Self-propelled goblin glider, sharpened forward fins, transthoracic entry left of the sternum, exiting posteriorly between scapula and spine. In a non-enhanced human this is uniformly fatal within minutes from cardiac tamponade, exsanguination, or tension pneumothorax. Subject survived via: (a) Formula-mediated cardiac and vascular resilience; (b) Formula-mediated hemostasis; (c) an unknown but plausibly Formula-enhanced capacity to maintain consciousness through hypovolemic shock long enough to be extracted by accomplices. The wound was operatively closed in a private European facility (file unrecovered). **Permanent residua**: a roughly stellate anterior chest scar and a corresponding posterior scar, both of which subject is documented to have shown to Harry in one of his crueler reveals, and which he covers reflexively when shirtless even in private (a rare somatic shame-tell). Healed pericardial adhesions are visible on the later scans. No functional cardiac compromise.

**Psychological impact of the impalement.** This is the medical event that authored the post-Clone-Saga Norman Osborn. The conviction — *I cannot be killed by him* — became foundational. The years in Europe were not recuperation; they were a long incubation of grandiose-restorative reorganization. He emerged believing himself genuinely beyond mortal containment, and the behavioral record since is consistent with that conviction.

**Repeated traumatic brain injuries.** Original Formula explosion (closed head trauma with probable diffuse axonal injury); the glider impact itself (subject hit the alley wall with his head before the glider reached Spider-Man); multiple concussive events across decades of combat with enhanced opponents; building collapse at Asgard during Siege (subject was recovered with depressed skull fracture, healed within weeks); pile-driver impact from Spider-Man at the climax of the Red Goblin arc; symbiote-mediated whiplash events. Cumulative TBI burden in a non-enhanced individual would have produced CTE-like dementia by the Stern era; in subject, the Formula's neurotrophic activity appears to repair gross structural injury without restoring premorbid inhibitory architecture — **he heals, but each repair leaves him slightly less inhibited than before, a one-way ratchet toward disinhibition that is independent of his characterological trajectory and additive to it.**

**Other significant injuries (selected):**
- Multiple rib fractures (combat-routine, healed without intervention).
- Right shoulder dislocation, recurrent, from glider-handling mechanics.
- Bilateral patellar tendonitis (chronic; the glider-stance is hard on the knees over thirty years).
- A through-and-through gunshot wound to the right thigh during a Bugle-era operation, healed without orthopedic intervention.
- Multiple lacerations and burns from his own pumpkin-bomb deployments; the dorsum of his left hand bears a faint reticular scar pattern from a mishandled incendiary in the Stern run.
- Bullet wound, occipital region, sustained during the late Spencer-era endgame, near-fatal in a normal physiology, survived with Formula assist.

## 4.6 Surgical History

- Tonsillectomy, childhood (routine).
- Right radius closed reduction, childhood (see §4.2).
- Post-impalement thoracic surgery, off-the-books European facility, mid-Bronze-Age publishing era (see §4.5).
- Cosmetic dental work, multiple sessions, across adulthood; the veneers are recent enough that they postdate his return to public life — vanity restored with the renewed audience.
- A series of self-administered or Oscorp-administered serum-modulation procedures across the Bendis/Brubaker era, including the implantation and removal of various sub-dermal monitoring and delivery devices during the HAMMER period — at one point subject had a Stark-derived diagnostic chip embedded subcutaneously over his left deltoid as part of the Iron Patriot interface, removed after Siege.
- Symbiote-extraction procedure post-Red Goblin, performed under extraordinary circumstances (the bonding had reached neural integration; extraction required combined biological, sonic, and surgical intervention). Residual: areas of focal hyper- and hypoesthesia along the trunk and forearms where symbiote tendrils had infiltrated; no functional motor deficit.
- The "Sin-Eater" purge: not a surgery in the conventional sense, but a quasi-mystical biochemical extraction of the Formula residue and, allegedly, of the Goblin's behavioral substrate. Produced temporary symptomatic remission. He sought re-corruption almost immediately. **The Sin-Eater episode is the cleanest natural experiment in the file** — it isolated the characterological from the chemical, and demonstrated that purified-Norman is still recognizably Norman: less grandiose, less violent, but still the man who lies about his father.

## 4.7 Substance Exposure Record

- **Alcohol**: heavy use age 18 to early 30s; abrupt cessation; near-abstinence since. The cessation is itself diagnostically interesting — it is not the trajectory of an addict in recovery but of a man for whom continued use became symbolically intolerable. He has never attended a meeting, never named the pattern, never spoken of it.
- **Tobacco**: socially, in the era when it was social; ceased early; no current use. Subject finds the smell of cigarette smoke on others mildly destabilizing — a probable Amberson-association, never acknowledged.
- **Caffeine**: heavy, sustained, lifelong. Black coffee, two to four cups before noon; espresso in the afternoon during high-load periods. He does not eat breakfast.
- **Prescription pharmaceuticals**: largely refused. Subject distrusts the prescriber relationship (it requires being a patient, which requires being smaller than someone else in a room). He has been documented as having been prescribed sleep agents, anxiolytics, and antipsychotics across various incarcerations; he has variously refused, palmed, hoarded for later use, or — in the HAMMER years — had his attending physician quietly reassigned.
- **Goblin Formula**: chronic, lifelong, ego-syntonic, identity-binding (see §4.4). The central substance fact of the file.
- **Carnage symbiote**: a 12-to-18-month bonded exposure during the Red Goblin period. Symbiote bonds are pharmacologically and neurologically comparable to a combined stimulant-opioid-psychedelic load with a parasitic intelligence layered on top; on subject's pre-existing dopaminergic dysregulation the effect was catastrophic and, paradoxically, *integrative* — for a period subject's Norman and Goblin presentations fused into a single, uniformly grandiose, uniformly sadistic operator, a state subject experienced as the truest version of himself. Post-extraction he has demonstrated occasional craving phenomena (anhedonia, somatic restlessness, references to "what we were") consistent with substance-bond withdrawal.
- **Demonic / Kindred-era exposures**: outside conventional medical taxonomy; produced memory editing, possibly synthetic memory implantation, and a period of behavioral apparent-remission that was almost certainly externally imposed rather than endogenous. The medical signature is the absence of expected somatic markers of his usual stress physiology — a man whose autonomic baseline was being held artificially low.

## 4.8 Dissociative-Amnesic Episodes

A careful longitudinal review distinguishes three classes of "Goblin amnesia":

1. **Genuine, serum- and stress-mediated dissociation** in the early period — subject genuinely could not recall the Goblin episodes for hours to days following decompensation, with retrograde reconstruction occurring over subsequent sleep cycles.
2. **Genuine, head-trauma-mediated amnesia** following the glider impact period — concussion-related, time-limited, organic.
3. **Feigned, instrumentally-deployed amnesia** in the post-Clone-Saga and HAMMER eras — by middle of the published record subject demonstrably can produce, suppress, and exploit "amnesia" at will for legal, social, and tactical benefit. Polygraph-equivalent assessments during HAMMER-era physicals were uniformly inconclusive because the underlying personality structure produces no autonomic guilt signature.

The medical record should therefore treat any claim by subject of amnesia for a violent act with maximum skepticism; the prior probability of feigning is now overwhelming.

## 4.9 Sensory, Perceptual, Endocrine

- **Vision**: enhanced; uncorrected 20/10; subject can read small print across a room and track flying objects at fastball-plus velocities. No documented strabismus, no documented color anomaly. Photosensitivity slightly elevated; he prefers warm low-Kelvin lighting in offices and is documented to dim conference rooms before sitting.
- **Hearing**: enhanced into the low ultrasonic; the cackling laugh of the Goblin includes harmonic content in a band most humans don't fully register — a probable explanation for why witnesses describe it as "wrong" beyond its content.
- **Olfaction**: enhanced; subject's documented aversion to certain perfumes (the gardenia note in particular — Emily Lyman wore gardenia) and to industrial solvents (Amberson worked with naphtha) suggests intact olfactory-limbic linkage to autobiographical memory.
- **Endocrine**: HPA axis chronically activated with paradoxically preserved diurnal cortisol curve — the Formula appears to have reset the regulatory set-point rather than abolished it. Testosterone in the upper end of normal range for a man twenty years younger. Insulin sensitivity preserved. Thyroid normal. **One unusual finding**: in the Stark BioMed scan, a small, indolent pituitary lesion of unclear significance was noted, recommended for follow-up, and never followed up.

## 4.10 Sleep, Pain, and Autonomic Baseline

Subject sleeps approximately four to five hours nightly, in two segments — a longer first segment, an arousal between 2:00 and 3:30 a.m., and a shorter second segment. The 2 a.m. arousal is lifelong, predates the Formula, and is the somatic residue of a childhood in which his father came home loudest in those hours. He uses the arousal productively: it is when most of his significant correspondence is dated. He does not dream much that he remembers; the dreams he does report (rarely, to physicians under duress, never to intimates) involve falling, fire, and a small green-tinted figure standing in a doorway. He has never asked anyone what they think the figure means.

Pain tolerance: extreme, partly Formula-mediated, partly characterological. He treats pain as informational rather than aversive, a trait observable in childhood survivors of physical abuse and reinforced in him by the Formula's analgesic side effect.

Autonomic baseline: resting heart rate in the low 50s, blood pressure controlled, respiration shallow at rest with a tendency to breath-holding under concentration (a tell — he stops breathing for several seconds when calculating a lie).

## 4.11 Latent and Prospective Medical Risks

- **Oncologic**: the Formula's telomerase-class activity and the chronic anabolic-stimulant endocrine profile place subject at non-trivial long-term risk for hematologic malignancy, hepatocellular carcinoma, and — given the pituitary finding — a slow-growing adenoma. His healing factor may mask early presentation until late stage.
- **Cardiovascular**: pericardial adhesions from the impalement; chronic sympathetic loading; the formula appears to remodel cardiac muscle but the long-tail risk of arrhythmia under extreme exertion or extre


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — OSBORN, NORMAN V.

*Granular bodily record. Compiled from longitudinal observation, photographic intake (Bugle archive, society pages, congressional record, HAMMER internal documentation, surveillance recovered post-Siege), combat footage, and reconstructed micro-behavior. State-dependent variants noted throughout under the headers BASELINE, MILD STRESS, ACUTE STRESS, GOBLIN-EMERGENT, INTIMACY/SEXUAL, and SLEEP/SOLITUDE. The body of this subject is a document of the two-self organization at the spine of the case file: nearly everything he does physically can be read as either the executive containing the Goblin or the Goblin leaking through the executive.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTION, FRAME, AND CARRIAGE

Subject is 5'11" and reads taller — a function of carriage rather than stature. Build is mesomorphic and disproportionate to chronological age: shoulders broad and squared, deltoids and trapezius hypertrophied beyond what his (largely sedentary) executive schedule would produce, latissimi visibly thickened when shirt is wet or fitted, waist narrow, hands and forearms disproportionately developed (the forearms in particular show veining and grip-musculature consistent with a man who routinely lifts loads well beyond civilian range). Resting heart rate observed in medical settings: 48–52, athlete range. Skin tone is high-color, with a persistent flush across the cheekbones and bridge of nose that intensifies under exertion or affect — a vascular tell of the chronic serum load. Body fat low and stable across decades; no observed seasonal fluctuation. There is no visible scar tissue across the sternum where the glider impalement occurred — the formula reabsorbs scarring — but on close inspection a faint keloidal seam runs paraspinal on the right, and a fine starburst pattern is visible at the right temple under direct light (original laboratory detonation).

**Carriage at BASELINE** is upright to the point of mannerism: shoulders back and slightly retracted, sternum lifted, chin neutral-to-elevated, weight forward over the balls of the feet. He stands as though always one beat from stepping toward someone. The default standing posture in conference and public-facing settings places the left hand in trouser pocket (rarely jacket pocket), thumb out, and the right hand free for gesture or contact — a deliberate asymmetry that frees the dominant hand and conveys ease. He does not lean on furniture. He does not slouch in chairs even in private; the spine remains off the seatback.

**Under MILD STRESS** the carriage tightens incrementally: the chin elevates two to three degrees, the shoulders retract further, and the standing weight shifts forward enough to bring the heels off-loaded. The hand leaves the pocket.

**Under ACUTE STRESS** carriage drops into a combat-ready set he does not appear to be aware of: feet square at hip-width, knees minutely unlocked, weight centered, hands free and slightly forward of the thighs. This posture is identical to the one captured on Avengers Tower footage immediately before the Siege of Asgard and to that visible in still frames from the Stacy bridge incident — a forty-year-stable threat-stance.

**GOBLIN-EMERGENT** posture is the photographic negative of the executive: spine flexes forward at the thoracolumbar junction into a hunched lean, shoulders roll forward and hike, the head juts on the cervical spine, elbows flare laterally, knees flex deeply, and weight rides the forefoot in a crouched, simian, pre-spring configuration. This is not the Goblin suit doing the work; the same posture appears when he is unarmored and decompensated.

---

## 2. GAIT, LOCOMOTION, AND USE OF SPACE

Walking gait at baseline is long-strided, heel-first, with minimal vertical oscillation — a tall man's walk performed by a not-quite-tall man. Cadence approximately 110 steps per minute, faster than corporate norm; subordinates trailing him are visibly hurried. Arm swing is asymmetric: the right arm swings noticeably less than the left, the right hand carried slightly forward and across the midline as if cradling something not present (this is a stable signature across decades — predates the Goblin armor and survives every change of costume; consistent with a habituated readiness to draw or throw).

He does not turn to address people he passes; he speaks over the shoulder without breaking pace, requiring them to keep up. In corridors he walks the centerline. In rooms he moves along walls until he selects a position, almost always with line-of-sight to the principal entrance and his back not fully exposed — a vigilance behavior continuous from the Bugle-ownership period through the HAMMER directorship. He sits with the same orientation: in restaurants, the back-to-wall corner; in offices, the chair angled so the door is in peripheral view.

On stairs he descends two at a time when unobserved, one at a time with a deliberate pause at landings when observed. He takes elevators alone when possible and stands in the back corner facing the doors, not against the side mirror. He does not use revolving doors if a hinged option exists.

**MILD STRESS** lengthens stride and accelerates cadence; the right arm's swing reduces further and the hand may rise to belt height.

**ACUTE STRESS** produces a peculiar smoothing: stride shortens, cadence becomes metronomic, and the walk acquires a gliding, knees-soft quality. Combat surveillance shows him moving toward an opponent with this same gait — it is the locomotor analogue of the calm that precedes his most dangerous behavior.

**GOBLIN-EMERGENT** gait is loose-jointed, bounding, and irregular: a step-and-a-half-skip pattern, frequent direction changes for no tactical reason, periodic crouches and springs. He laughs while moving. He covers ground in this state faster than in his executive walk despite the apparent inefficiency.

---

## 3. THE HANDS

The hands are the most informative single region. Long-fingered, broad-palmed, with prominent extensor tendons; nails kept short, square, and buffed (never glossed). A faint chemical staining is intermittently visible at the cuticles of the right index and middle fingers — solvent residue from personal benchwork he refuses to delegate.

**Gesture vocabulary at BASELINE:** he speaks with the right hand primarily, palm-down for assertion (a dominance gesture he uses three to four times more than the population baseline), palm-up only in calculated displays of openness (deal-closing, press conferences with a particular kind of audience). The "steeple" — fingertips of both hands touched at chest height — is his default thinking posture in seated meetings and is held for unusually long intervals (15–40 seconds) without micro-movement, a stillness most people cannot sustain. When listening to a subordinate he disapproves of, the right index finger taps the desk in groups of three, pauses, three, pauses — a metric pattern that subordinates have learned to dread.

He touches his own face rarely (low for a man of his cognitive load), but when he does, the gesture is specific: the pad of the right thumb to the philtrum, index curled across the upper lip, a brief downward drag. This is his concealment-of-smile gesture and is the single most reliable tell that he is amused by something he should not be amused by — typically another person's distress.

He shakes hands with deliberate over-pressure on first contact (~30–40% above conversational norm), held one beat longer than expected, with the left hand frequently capping the joined hands at the wrist (not the elbow — the elbow-cap he reserves for performances of paternal warmth, e.g., with Harry in photographs, with Lily Hollister early, with the Dark Avengers roster on introduction). Release is sudden.

**Under MILD STRESS** the hands begin to occupy themselves with objects: pen rotated between thumb and index in lazy figure-eights; cufflink turned; wedding band absent (never worn after Emily's death) but the bare ring finger of the left hand is rubbed by the thumb in moments of unguarded reflection — a forty-year ghost-ring behavior.

**Under ACUTE STRESS** the hands still. This is counter-intuitive and important. Most people's hands accelerate under pressure; his slow and then arrest. The steeple deepens; the fingers whiten at the tips from pressure. When the hands move again, they move once and decisively.

**GOBLIN-EMERGENT:** the hands open wide, fingers splayed and clawed, and the gesture vocabulary becomes operatic — sweeping arcs, throwing motions even when nothing is being thrown, the conductor's downbeat to punctuate a laugh. The right hand develops a small pre-throw rehearsal twitch at the wrist that observers have identified seconds before pumpkin-bomb deployments.

**INTIMACY:** with sexual partners, the hand pattern is acquisitive — palm placed flat on the small of the back, sliding to the hip, lingering; with women whose status he wishes to convert, he uses the wrist-cap handshake variant in the first encounter and reproduces it in the first physical approach. There is no observed soft or exploratory touch in his repertoire. He does not stroke; he places.

---

## 4. FACE, EYES, AND VOCAL APPARATUS

The face is long-jawed, high-cheekboned, with a prominent supraorbital ridge that shadows the eyes from above in most lighting. Hair is auburn-going-rust, kept full and back-swept, with a sharp side part on the left held with light pomade; the hairline has not receded materially in thirty years of publication time (serum). When he runs the right hand through it — a stress behavior — it falls back almost perfectly into place, which he knows.

The eyes are the most-photographed feature and the one most studied by his subordinates. Iris green-hazel, sclera slightly hyperemic at baseline (vascular signature of the formula), pupil response brisk and often disproportionate to ambient light — under affective load his pupils dilate visibly even in bright settings, a tell that some have learned to read (Bendis-era Maria Hill referenced it in debrief). His blink rate is low at baseline (8–11 per minute, against population norm of 15–20). Under stress it drops further; in full Goblin emergence it can disappear for fifteen-second stretches.

**Eye-contact pattern.** Predatory-prolonged with peers and rivals: holds gaze through the social break-point and into the discomfort threshold, then withdraws on his own timing, not theirs. With subordinates he uses brief, scything glances — a half-second lock followed by complete dismissal — a gesture experienced by recipients as a small physical impact. With Harry, surveillance footage and family photographs document an entirely different pattern: gaze drops to the middle distance below the son's face, returns, drops again. He cannot sustain direct eye contact with his son for more than three seconds in non-performative settings. He can sustain it indefinitely in photographs.

**The mouth.** At rest the lips are thin and held in a near-neutral line with a slight downward turn at the corners — what a stranger reads as severity and a familiar reads as the suppression of contempt. The smile vocabulary is specific and worth cataloging:
- *Press smile:* symmetrical, teeth shown, eyes crinkled in performed warmth. Held three to four seconds and dropped instantly. The drop is the tell — the muscle release is total and immediate, with no residual warmth in transition.
- *Boardroom smile:* asymmetric, right corner higher, no teeth, eyes uninvolved. Indicates he has won something he is not yet announcing.
- *Contempt smile:* left corner higher, single brief flash, accompanied by a one-beat nasal exhalation. Directed at people he has decided are beneath him; he is rarely aware he is producing it.
- *Goblin smile:* full dentition, gums shown, eyes wide rather than crinkled, held without modulation. Appears in Norman-presentation only at moments of catastrophic decompensation and is the single most reliable warning sign that the executive is gone.

**The laugh.** Three discriminable laughs across the record. The social laugh is a brief, throaty, two-syllable concession ("heh-heh") used to lubricate conversation and not repeated. The genuine-amused laugh — rare — is a quieter, lower, almost private chuckle that he tries to suppress with the philtrum-thumb gesture above. The Goblin laugh is the discharge phenomenon: high-pitched, glottal, cascading in irregular bursts of seven to fifteen syllables, head thrown back, mouth wide, often accompanied by tears at the lateral canthi. It emerges only under severe affective overload and is medically a release valve. It is also infectious to itself — once initiated, it tends to re-trigger across several minutes.

**Voice.** Baseline pitch mid-baritone, resonance forward and nasal-edged, articulation crisp with an Eastern boarding-school overlay (clipped final consonants, fully voiced ‹r›, a faint dental ‹t›). Volume modulation is unusually wide: he can drop to a near-whisper that compels listeners to lean in (a dominance technique he employs with hostile interlocutors) and lift without strain to a podium-projecting full voice. Cadence at baseline is measured, with deliberate pauses at the ends of clauses he wants weighted. Under acute stress the cadence smooths and the volume drops — the dangerous voice is the quiet one. Under Goblin emergence the voice climbs in pitch and breaks into a sing-song delivery with extended vowels and grotesque enunciation, occasionally rhyming. The transition between executive voice and Goblin voice can occur mid-sentence and is one of the most reliably destabilizing experiences his subordinates report.

---

## 5. GROOMING, DRESS, AND OBJECT RELATIONS

Grooming is exact and time-stable. He shaves twice daily (morning and pre-evening) with a straight razor he sharpens himself — a ritual that occupies twelve to fourteen minutes of his morning and during which he is observed (HAMMER residential surveillance) to mouth conversations silently, rehearsing the day's confrontations. The shave is performed shirtless, in front of a mirror, with the door open behind him — never with the door closed. He does not nick himself; the formula's reflex enhancement is incidentally protective.

Hair is washed daily, conditioned, combed wet and re-set as it dries. Nails are clipped weekly (Sunday evenings) and buffed; he does not visit a manicurist. Cologne is sparing — a single dry, citrus-vetiver applied to the throat only, never the wrists. He brushes his teeth four times daily and carries a small palladium-cased toothpick for use after meals, employed privately. Breath at conversational range is consistently neutral.

**Wardrobe.** Bespoke, Savile Row in the Bugle-ownership and Dark Reign eras, with a consistent palette: charcoal, slate, oxblood, forest. Shirt collars cut wide to accommodate the throat. Pocket squares present but unflashy, folded in a flat presidential rather than a peaked or puff configuration. Ties are silk, restrained pattern, knotted in a half-Windsor with a deliberate dimple. Cufflinks are the one indulgence — varied, often subtly thematic (a small lab-glass beaker pair he wears on board-meeting days he intends to be hostile). Shoes are black or oxblood captoe oxfords, mirror-polished, replaced rather than repaired. There is no observed casual wardrobe of consequence; even in residential surveillance footage he is in tailored trousers and shirt sleeves at minimum. Pajamas are silk, dark.

**Object handling.** He is acquisitive but not fidgety with objects. He picks up the things in another person's office without asking and replaces them rotated thirty degrees from their original orientation — a small dominance behavior whose frequency he is probably not aware of. He drinks from glassware with the right hand, the left hand cradling the base; he never holds a cup by the handle.

**The armor.** The Goblin suit and, later, the Iron Patriot armor function as extensions of body and require listing here as somatic objects rather than equipment. The Goblin suit he dons in a particular order beginning with the gloves (a sequence aficionados of his surveillance know to flag — gloves first means he intends to use his hands intimately). The Iron Patriot armor he wore as a near-constant second skin during Dark Reign, sleeping in residential proximity to its rack, and the dismounting ritual at end of day was protracted (forty-plus minutes), suggesting a difficulty separating from it. After Siege, in custody, he was observed reaching for the absent gauntlet repeatedly — a phantom-limb behavior.

---

## 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Total sleep at baseline is four to five hours per night, achieved without apparent functional impairment (serum-mediated). Onset latency is short (under ten minutes). He sleeps supine, hands at sides or one hand on the abdomen, head centered on the pillow — a corpse-like configuration he maintains through the night with minimal positional change. He does not snore. Respiration is slow and even at twelve to fourteen breaths per minute.

REM intrusion is documented as vivid and disturbed; HAMMER medical recorded sleep talking in approximately a quarter of monitored nights, with content clustering around three themes: instructions to an unseen subordinate ("hold him — hold him there"), addresses to his father in a register he never uses awake (placating, then defiant), and, most often, a one-sided conversation with Peter Parker conducted in a near-whisper. He wakes at 0445–0500 without alarm, sits upright, places both feet on the floor simultaneously, and is operational within ninety seconds.

**Under stress** sleep compresses to two to three hours and onset latency disappears entirely; he is observed to fall asleep mid-paperwork at his desk for twenty- to forty-minute intervals and to wake with full executive function. **Under Goblin emergence** he may not sleep at all for forty-eight to seventy-two hours; the crash that follows is profound and produces twelve- to sixteen-hour sleeps from which he wakes disoriented and dangerous.

He requires the bedroom door to be closed and the window operable — a child's strategy retained.

---

## 7. EATING, DRINKING, ORAL PATTERNS

Eating is fueling, not enjoyment. He prefers small, dense, high-protein meals taken alone or while reading; he dislikes long banquets and visibly accelerates the pace of restaurant meals when trapped in them. He uses the European cutlery hold (knife perpetually in right hand, fork in left, tines down), cuts each bite as he eats it rather than in advance, and never speaks with food in his mouth — a hyper-controlled oral discipline that contrasts with the Goblin presentation's oral excess.

Preferences: rare steak, raw oysters, dark chocolate, black coffee, single-malt scotch (Islay, peated). Aversions: anything sweet to excess, anything garnished, anything served family-style. He does not eat dessert in public. He drinks scotch in three-finger measures, neat, with a single ice cube he watches melt rather than swirl. Wine he affects to know about and selects by price tier rather than palate.

Alcohol tolerance is high (serum-mediated metabolism); intoxication is rare and, when observed, presents as increased volume, slower speech, and a pronounced contemptuous edge — not loosened warmth. He does not smoke; he watches others smoke with mild distaste. He chews ice when alone and reading, a fragmenting molar habit that produces a distinctive sound those who have shared a household with him remember.

The oral signature under Goblin emergence reverses the discipline entirely: open mouth, tongue visible at the lower lip during exertion, audible breathing, occasional drool at the right corner.

---

## 8. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE PATTERNS

The sexual record is sparse but consistent. After Emily Lyman's death, no documented sustained pair-bond; partners are acquired, used, and discarded, with a marked preference for women significantly younger than himself and proximate to people he wishes to wound (the Hollister pattern; the inferential Stacy pattern). Approach behavior is direct and asymmetric — he does not court. He invites; the invitation contains an assumption.

Physical pattern with partners reports as: intense, controlling, brief in duration of the act, abrupt in disengagement. He does not sleep with partners; he leaves or arranges for them to leave. Aftercare is absent. Affection in the post-coital window is replaced by conversation about the partner's life that has the texture of debrief — what they know, who they know, what they want. This is one of the most consistent reports across decades and partners.

There is no observed pornographic or paraphilic pattern of note. The sadistic impulse is satisfied elsewhere — in business, in combat, in the Parker campaign — and does not appear to seek a sexual channel. Sexuality is, for him, primarily a means of access (to information, to status, to wounding a rival through the partner) rather than a primary pleasure.

The closest he comes to observed tenderness is with infants in photographed settings: he holds them correctly, attentively, and a faint authentic softness crosses the face that is absent everywhere else. The softness lasts seconds. With his own grandson, the same pattern; with Harry as an adult, never.

---

## 9. AUTONOMIC AND MICRO-SIGNATURE TELLS

A catalogue of the smaller, harder-to-suppress somatic phenomena:

- **The jaw clench at the masseter.** Visible as a small bilateral bulge below the zygomatic arch when he is constraining a response. Bilateral indicates suppression of speech; unilateral right indicates suppression of a smile.
- **The throat clearing in threes.** Under conversational pressure he clears his throat in groups of three with a half-second between, never in singles or pairs. Frequency rises sharply when he is about to lie about something that matters to him personally (the Harry-related lies; the father-related lies).
- **The right-eyebrow lift.** A single sharp elevation of the right brow accompanying a downward chin tuck — his "I have heard you, and you have made an error" gesture. Subordinates have learned that this is the last warning before professional consequences.
- **The nostril flare on inhale.** Bilateral, brief, accompanies the first wave of anger. He often interrupts it by speaking.
- **The right-hand tremor.** A fine intention tremor of the right hand appears when the serum is overdue — three to six hours past optimal dose. It is undetectable at conversational distance but visible on close inspection at the fingertips when he extends the hand to gesture. He notices it and pockets the hand. This is the most reliable indicator that he is approaching a re-dose window.
- **The left-temple pulse.** Becomes visible when systolic pressure climbs. Combat footage shows it preceding Goblin emergence by several minutes.
- **The swallow before naming.** Before speaking the names "Peter," "Harry," "Spider-Man," or "father," a small dry swallow is observable. The latency before the name itself is fractionally longer than for other names. Four words; one body knows them.
- **The right-shoulder roll.** A single small backward roll of the right shoulder, often preceding decisive physical action. In combat footage it precedes by approximately 1.2 seconds the throw of a pumpkin bomb or the initiation of glider acceleration. In the board


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

*Section 7-A of the longitudinal file. Cross-reference Sections 1 (History), 3 (Psychological), 5 (Personality). All relational behaviors keyed to canon instances and modeled forward as predictive templates.*

---

## 7-A.1 — Attachment Classification and Developmental Substrate

Subject's attachment organization is best classified as **disorganized-controlling, punitive subtype, with secondary compulsive-self-reliance overlay**. The classification is not provisional; it is the single most stable finding in the entire file, observable in every dyad subject has formed from age seven (earliest narrated memory, *Spectacular Spider-Man* #178–180, DeMatteis) through the present.

The developmental substrate is documented and consistent across writers:

- **Amberson Osborn** — the father — provided what attachment theorists call *frightened/frightening* caregiving. He was simultaneously the source of resources (food, shelter, identity, the family name) and the source of terror (beatings, verbal degradation, drunken unpredictability). The infant/child cannot resolve this paradox; the attachment system activates toward the very figure it must flee. The behavioral residue in adulthood is a chronic inability to distinguish *protection* from *predation* in close others — every intimate must be tested for which they really are, and the test never concludes.
- **Emily Osborn** — the mother — died early enough to leave no remediating internal object. There is no soft voice in Norman's head. Every later female intimate is approached without a template for benign female regard, which is why those relationships collapse so reliably into instrumentalization (Lily Hollister), grooming-displacement (the *Sins Past* material), or projective rivalry (Emma Frost, Lindsay McCabe-adjacent figures across the Bendis run).
- **No documented allo-parental buffer.** No surviving aunt, nanny, teacher, or clergyman appears in the canonical childhood. Subject grew up inside the dyad with Amberson, with no third term. This absence explains the lifelong difficulty tolerating triadic relationships: he can do dyads (rival, son, lieutenant) but cannot sustain a stable triangle — when a third person enters, he splits the field and destroys one leg of it.

The resolution strategy, locked in by middle adolescence, is the classic *identification with the aggressor with a vow of inversion*: **I will become my father's strength and never his weakness; I will inflict, never receive; I will be witnessed and feared, never witnessed and pitied.** This vow is the engine of every adult relationship in the record.

---

## 7-A.2 — The Bonding Sequence (Idealize → Use → Test → Devalue → Destroy)

Subject does not form attachments in the ordinary sense. He *recruits* objects through a five-stage sequence so consistent across the canon that it functions as a fingerprint.

**Stage 1 — Idealization / Recruitment.** Subject identifies an object of interest (mentor, lieutenant, lover, son's friend, rival, eventually a nation) and deploys what observers describe as genuine, almost startling charisma: undivided attention, perfectly-calibrated flattery, generous material gifts, intellectual seriousness, the implication of inheritance. He is, in this phase, *legitimately good company* — this is the file's most operationally important warning. Documented exemplars: his courtship of Mendel Stromm (mentor stage, pre-betrayal); his initial cultivation of the Hobgoblin candidates; his ingratiation of the Avengers' civilian liaisons during Dark Reign; his early Iron Patriot press pool. The idealization is not faked in the cynical sense — subject genuinely experiences a charge of admiration for the object's utility-to-him, and this charge is felt by the object as love.

**Stage 2 — Use.** The object is integrated into a project. Subject extracts value: Stromm's formula, Harry's loyalty as heir-apparent, Menken's legal cover, Lily Hollister's body and political utility, Victoria Hand's competence, the Sentry's power, Spider-Man's existence as foil. During this phase subject's executive functioning is at its highest; he is a *good* manager of people he is currently using.

**Stage 3 — Test.** Subject probes the object for the precise vulnerability he intends later to exploit. Tests take the form of small humiliations, inconsistent reinforcement schedules, sudden withdrawals of approval followed by lavish reinstatement, and pointed questions about loyalty. Harry's entire childhood is a single sustained Stage 3. The Dark Avengers were tested individually and constantly (Bullseye's leash; Daken's identity-baiting; Moonstone's seductions tolerated and then weaponized). The test is not strategic only — it is also affective; subject is checking whether the object will become the despised, the contemptible, the *prey*. He hopes simultaneously that they will and that they will not.

**Stage 4 — Devaluation.** The object inevitably fails the test (the test is designed to be failed). Subject experiences a contempt-flush — physiological as well as psychological; the lip lifts, the breath shortens, the voice drops. The object is reclassified from asset to instrument-to-be-discarded. This is often invisible to the object, who continues to operate under Stage 2 conditions for weeks or months.

**Stage 5 — Destruction.** Subject removes the object, almost always with theatrical signature. Stromm goes to prison via subject's own evidence. Hollister is publicly exposed and her child appropriated. Gwen Stacy is thrown from a bridge. Harry is faked-dead, resurrected, disinherited, re-cultivated, re-discarded. The Sentry is dispatched at Siege the moment his utility expires. The destruction is rarely silent; subject requires the object to *know they were beaten by him specifically*, and ideally requires a third party to witness.

The cycle's mean length varies — minutes for sycophants, decades for Spider-Man — but the structure does not vary.

---

## 7-A.3 — Distrust as Baseline, Trust as Tactical Loan

Subject does not "trust" in the felt sense. He extends what is better termed **operational credit**: a calculated, time-limited, monitored grant of latitude to a counterparty, withdrawable without notice. He maintains, by inference from his behavior, an internal ledger on every significant relation: what they owe, what they've cost, what they could cost, what leverage he holds on them. This ledger is consulted constantly; it is the closest he comes to thinking about people.
