If the error repeats, the assistant is gone within the pay period, but with a generous severance and a glowing letter — preserving his reputation as a reasonable man while ensuring she never works in his industry again. *(High confidence. Substrate: documented Menken-class subordinate management.)*

**GIVEN** a junior engineer presents him with a genuinely novel idea → **EXPECT** a brief, real warmth: he leans forward, asks two or three sharp follow-ups, names a date by which he wants the prototype. The engineer will leave the room elated. Within six months one of three things will have happened: the engineer is being groomed for an executive role (idealization phase, the dangerous one); the engineer's idea has been quietly transferred to a different division under different attribution; or the engineer has been pushed onto a project designed to fail in order to neutralize a potential rival. Which of the three depends on whether the idea threatens subject's primacy in his own house. *(High confidence. Substrate: Stromm pattern, repeated.)*

**GIVEN** a board meeting → **EXPECT** he arrives two minutes early, never first (first is eager) and never last (last is theater he does not need on his own boards), and takes the same seat. He speaks last on every agenda item; he watches faces during others' speech and writes nothing down — note-taking is delegated. He memorizes positions and uses them in side conversations after the meeting. He praises publicly with restraint and criticizes privately with surgical specificity. The few times he criticizes publicly, the target is being removed; the public criticism IS the removal. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** an employee asks for personal leave for a family matter → **EXPECT** instant approval, delivered with an unforced sympathy that confuses anyone expecting otherwise. He will remember the detail (the daughter's surgery, the parent's death) and ask after it on the employee's return. The kindness is real in the moment and instrumental in the aggregate; the employee will work harder for him for years. This is the deepest danger of him — that the warmth is not always faked, only always usable. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a security guard fails to recognize him at his own building → **EXPECT** he is pleased. He will not say so. He will compliment the guard's protocol-adherence to the head of security and inquire by name about the guard later. The guard will be promoted. This is one of the few unambiguous goods subject does, and he does it because it confirms his own taste in standards, not because of the guard. *(Moderate-high confidence.)*

---

## 7a.6 — CHARITY, PHILANTHROPY, PUBLIC-FACING WARMTH

**GIVEN** a charity gala in his honor → **EXPECT** he attends, gives a check larger than expected, speaks for four minutes without notes, mentions his late wife once and his son not at all, and leaves before the dessert course on a fabricated call. The four minutes will contain one genuinely affecting sentence about a cause he in fact does not care about, delivered with full apparent sincerity. The check will be tax-structured to cost him a third of its face value. He will know the names of three children in the cause's promotional material and use them. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** he is asked to fund pediatric medical research → **EXPECT** he funds it. Generously. The Emily Lyman wing of somewhere exists or will exist. This is one of the few categories where the giving is not purely instrumental — there is a thread of unfinished business with his wife's death that pediatric research touches. He will not examine the thread. *(Moderate confidence, inferential.)*

**GIVEN** he is asked to fund mental health, addiction, or family-violence services → **EXPECT** refusal phrased as portfolio focus. These are categories where the giving would require an admission to himself that he cannot make. *(Moderate-high confidence.)*

---

## 7a.7 — WOMEN, INTIMACY, SEXUALITY

**GIVEN** a romantic or sexual interest → **EXPECT** he pursues it like an acquisition: research the target's circumstances, identify the lack she does not name, supply it, escalate access, withdraw selectively to induce pursuit. Beauty matters less than usefulness-plus-vulnerability; the Lily Hollister pattern (younger, ambitious, politically positioned, father-wounded) is the template. He is not impotent and not promiscuous; the affairs are few, intense, instrumental, and discarded. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a woman in his life expresses an emotional need he has not anticipated → **EXPECT** withdrawal, then contempt expressed as concern ("you seem unwell — perhaps you need rest"). Genuine emotional demand collapses the idealization phase; he cannot tolerate being the recipient of need without converting the need-bearer into a dependent and thereby a despised object. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a woman is unmoved by him → **EXPECT** sustained, polite, escalating attention until she is moved or she is destroyed. Indifference from women, as from rivals, is the form of injury he metabolizes worst. He will not assault; he will manipulate the woman's circumstances — her job, her partner, her family — until she has reason to engage. *(High confidence, inferential.)*

**GIVEN** intimacy itself → **EXPECT** he sleeps in a separate bed when possible. He does not share a bathroom. He does not undress in front of partners. The body the formula gave him is also the body Amberson hit; the privacy is not modesty. *(Moderate confidence, inferential.)*

---

## 7a.8 — CHILDREN, GRANDCHILDREN, OTHER PEOPLE'S OFFSPRING

**GIVEN** he is alone in a room with a child not his own → **EXPECT** unsettling competence. He will speak to a seven-year-old as he speaks to a director, with respect and full attention, ask one or two questions that take the child seriously, and produce in the child the lifelong memory of having been *seen*. He is not interested in the child sexually or sentimentally; he is interested in the child's response to being addressed as an adult, because that response is data about future raw material. *(Moderate-high confidence.)*

**GIVEN** Normie Osborn (his grandson) → **EXPECT** wild oscillation. Idealization phases ("he is the future of the line, the corrected Harry") followed by sudden coldness when the child shows a behavior coded as weak. He will buy the child an inappropriate gift (an heirloom watch at age eight; a small handgun, properly secured, at twelve) and watch closely how it is received. The child's mother will be cut out of decision loops repeatedly. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** an infant cries in his presence → **EXPECT** immediate, visible discomfort, smoothed within a second. He associates infant cry with Emily's death and Harry's existence and the conjunction of the two. He will leave the room within five minutes on a constructed pretext. *(High confidence, inferential. Substrate: blame-the-infant pattern with Harry.)*

---

## 7a.9 — MEDIA, PRESS, PUBLIC SPEAKING

**GIVEN** a hostile press interview → **EXPECT** he begins by complimenting the interviewer's previous work (specific, accurate, slightly flattering), reframes the first hostile question into a question he wanted asked, and answers the rephrased version with controlled candor. He never says "no comment." He uses the interviewer's first name three times in the first ten minutes. He laughs once, briefly, at his own expense — a calibrated micro-display of humility designed to inoculate against the larger arrogance the interview will eventually expose. If the interviewer holds the line, the temperature drops, and a single sentence near the end will land as a threat the interviewer cannot quote without sounding paranoid. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a friendly press event → **EXPECT** less effort, more visible boredom controlled to a half-smile. He does not need to manage friendly press; he needs only to not insult them, and he calibrates exactly to that floor. *(Moderate confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a televised crisis address → **EXPECT** dark suit, American flag in left frame (always left — the eye's natural first stop), hands visible on the desk or lectern, no notes, eye contact direct into the lens. He will use the word "we" until the address's emotional pivot, then switch to "I" for the commitment. The pivot is rehearsed. The Iron Patriot phase was an unbroken three-hundred-day version of this address; the technique is durable. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a heckler at a public event → **EXPECT** he engages, briefly, with apparent humor. He will get the room's laugh. The heckler will be identified by security and a file initiated within the hour; depending on the heckler's profile, the response ranges from a job offer (co-opt the threat) to a sustained civil harassment via proxy. *(High confidence.)*

---

## 7a.10 — PEERS, RIVALS, POWERFUL MEN

**GIVEN** a room with Tony Stark → **EXPECT** sustained, low-key needling beneath an apparent civility. He will compliment Stark's most recent technical achievement with a specificity that demonstrates he has read the patent filings, then ask a question whose only honest answer reveals a flaw Stark has not publicly acknowledged. The two will not be alone in the room if subject can help it; the performance requires witnesses. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a room with Doctor Doom → **EXPECT** stiff, almost formal mutual recognition between two malignant narcissists who have correctly diagnosed each other and who know the other has correctly diagnosed them. Conversation will be brief, mostly silent, oddly companionable. Neither will attack the other in that room. Both will leave it planning. *(High confidence. Substrate: Dark Reign Cabal dynamics.)*

**GIVEN** a room with a sitting U.S. president → **EXPECT** deference precisely calibrated to camera presence. Off camera, he is the room's actual center and the president knows it. He addresses the president by title once at greeting, then drops the title for the rest of the conversation — a small, deliberate erosion. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a room with Reed Richards or Hank McCoy or any peer scientist who out-credentials him → **EXPECT** technical conversation pitched at exactly the depth that requires the peer to acknowledge his competence without conceding superiority. He will introduce one piece of original work into the conversation that the peer has not seen. If the peer dismisses it, he files the dismissal. If the peer engages, he engages back, and a brief authentic intellectual pleasure shows on his face before he closes it. *(High confidence.)*

---

## 7a.11 — STRANGERS, SERVICE WORKERS, THE CITY

**GIVEN** a server, valet, doorman, or driver → **EXPECT** courtesy. He tips generously, addresses by name when the name is visible, and remembers preferences across visits. This is partly genuine class-performance (the man Amberson was not), partly instrumental (the staff who like him will warn him of what they see), and entirely consistent. Subordinates love him until the moment they become rivals. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** an aggressive panhandler or street confrontation → **EXPECT** the formula-augmented man inside the suit takes a half-step forward before the executive reasserts. The aggressor will read the half-step and disengage; the executive will continue walking as if nothing happened. The face at that moment is the closest a stranger will come to seeing the Goblin without the costume. *(High confidence.)*

**GIVEN** a young woman in public distress that he could trivially assist (a fall, lost child, medical episode) → **EXPECT** he assists, competently, with a calm that calms the scene. He will give his real first name and a fictional surname or no surname. He will not wait for thanks. The act is real; the obscuring of identity is reflexive; the warmth in his chest when he walks away is one of the few feelings he allows himself unstudied. *(Moderate confidence, inferential — the substrate is the rare moments of unsought paternal affect toward Harry.)*

---

## 7a.12 — RECREATION, ART, CULTURE

**GIVEN** unscheduled cultural intake → **EXPECT** opera, specifically Wagner and late Verdi; he attends in a private box; he weeps once or twice per season and never lets anyone see it. He reads history (military, dynastic) and biography; he does not read fiction (fiction asks him to inhabit other selves, which he refuses). He collects, in a controlled way: rare scientific instruments, Edison-era and earlier, displayed in his study. *(Moderate-high confidence.)*

**GIVEN** sport → **EXPECT** he watches boxing (one-on-one, no team obfuscation of individual will), follows it knowledgeably, and has corner-side seats at major fights. He does not play golf despite the social utility; the speed is wrong for his metabolism. He sails alone when he can. *(Moderate confidence, inferential.)*

**GIVEN** music in his own residence → **EXPECT** classical, mid-volume, frequently the same handful of recordings (a specific Karajan


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

*High-stakes behavioral forecasting. Format: GIVEN [stimulus condition, specified to operational granularity] → EXPECT [predicted response, with timing, somatic markers, escalation path, and containment notes]. Predictions are derived from the longitudinal pattern documented in Sections 1–5 and reflect the convergence of the malignant-narcissistic spine, the formula-mediated decompensation profile, and the Amberson-substrate wound. Confidence-graded where the record is sparse.*

---

## 6.1 — THE CORE WOUND ARCHITECTURE (orienting note)

Before tabulating stimulus-response pairs: the wound is not a single locus. It is a layered structure, and predictions vary by which layer a given stimulus penetrates. From most superficial to most foundational:

- **Layer 1 — The Executive Vanity.** Threat to the public-competent-Osborn presentation (business loss, social slight, being out-argued in a room of peers). Cheap to provoke, cheap to contain. Responses are calculated and verbal.
- **Layer 2 — The Rivalry Axis.** Anything that registers as "another man is larger than me in the space I claim." Triggers obsessional planning, displacement onto subordinates, increased serum titration.
- **Layer 3 — The Spectacle Need.** Threat to being witnessed — denial of audience, mockery in lieu of fear, indifference. Provokes increasingly baroque acts designed to *force* witness.
- **Layer 4 — The Harry Channel.** Anything that reactivates the failed-father / failed-son loop. Penetrates faster than any other stimulus; produces affect he cannot fully script.
- **Layer 5 — The Amberson Substrate.** Direct contact with the helpless-beaten-child self-state — through humiliation, physical restraint, paternal comparison, or the experience of being smaller than another man in a way he cannot reframe. This is the load-bearing wound. Stimuli that reach Layer 5 produce the catastrophic regression profile: full Goblin emergence, suicidal-grandiose gestures, and the discharge laugh.

Read every prediction below as: *which layer does this stimulus reach, and how fast does the chain unwind from there.*

---

## 6.2 — DIRECT PHYSICAL THREAT

**GIVEN: an unenhanced operator (e.g. SHIELD strike team, masked vigilante without superhuman attribute) brings him to point-blank gunpoint in private, no witnesses.**
EXPECT: immediate Layer 1–2 response, executive presentation dominant. Slowed breathing within four to six seconds (he has done this before; the autonomic startle is brief). He will speak first and at length — a verbal counter-pressure tactic, designed to (a) identify the operator's chain of command, (b) locate the operator's wound (the operator's son, mortgage, dead partner, ideological vanity — he reads people fast), and (c) offer something. Bribes will be sequenced: legitimate (money), then transgressive (information on a colleague), then identity-violating (the operator's own pathology named aloud). If the operator does not fire within the first ninety seconds of speech, subject's probability of survival approaches one. The Goblin does not emerge in this scenario; this is the kind of pressure he was built for.

**GIVEN: the same operator brings him to gunpoint in front of a watching crowd, with cameras.**
EXPECT: an entirely different response. Spectacle availability flips the calculation. He will not bargain; he will *perform* the bargaining-refusal. Expect a controlled smile, an open-palm gesture, and a statement designed to humiliate the operator on the record ("Go ahead. The footage will outlive both of us. Your mother will see it"). The play is to convert the operator's act, executed or not, into a humiliation of the operator. Containment note: never threaten him with cameras running unless prepared to follow through; performative threat in public *strengthens* him.

**GIVEN: a superhuman of his power-tier (Spider-Man, Iron Man, Captain America) physically dominates him in combat to the point of restraint, in a non-lethal manner.**
EXPECT: Layer 5 contact. Restraint — the somatic posture of being pinned, immobilized, talked-down-to from above — is the Amberson posture. Expect the laugh within thirty seconds. Expect verbal output to become rapid, glossolalic, sexualized-aggressive toward the restrainer ("Is this what you wanted? Is this what you needed to feel?"). Expect a sudden, surprising attempt at self-injury or environment-injury to break the moment — biting through his own cheek, headbutting the floor, triggering a hidden incendiary on his person. The goal is not escape; the goal is the rupture of the immobilized-child tableau. After the moment passes, expect either dissociative flatness or a full Goblin emergence depending on whether spectators remain.

**GIVEN: lethal force is used against him and he survives by formula-mediated healing, in private.**
EXPECT: a multi-year planning operation against the attacker, modeled on the Clone Saga template. The attacker becomes a candidate for the Parker-position in his psyche; he will study them, infiltrate their intimates, and engineer a sustained psychological dismantling rather than a counter-killing. Counter-killing would be too small. Containment note: anyone who has tried to kill Osborn and survived must be assumed to be under longitudinal surveillance until his death is verified.

---

## 6.3 — BETRAYAL BY SUBORDINATES

**GIVEN: a vetted lieutenant (Menken-class, the deputy who has demonstrated sycophantic loyalty over years) defects with documents to a federal agency or rival.**
EXPECT: a brief, observable freeze (two to four seconds, eye-blink rate drops, jaw locks) — the genuine narcissistic injury, immediately suppressed. Within the first hour: cold planning mode. He will not contact the defector directly. He will contact three peripheral figures in the defector's life — a sibling, an ex-spouse, a college acquaintance — and offer or threaten in ways calibrated to make the defector's subsequent testimony unstable. Within twenty-four hours: a public statement of generous regret ("I am disappointed but I wish him well"), which is operational camouflage. Within ninety days: the defector will experience a discrediting event (a planted indiscretion, a financial irregularity surfaced from old records, a leaked recording). Direct violence is *not* the default in this scenario; he prefers the defector alive, ruined, and visibly so, as instruction to remaining staff.

**GIVEN: a Dark-Avengers-tier asset (a known unstable killer he has weaponized) defects or turns on him operationally.**
EXPECT: a different response — closer to a lion-handler's reflex than a CEO's. He will not be surprised; he priced this in at recruitment. He will have a pre-built kill-switch (chemical, biometric, leverage on a hostage relationship) and will use it without preamble. No speech, no offer, no spectacle. This is one of the few scenarios in which he acts with pure instrumental efficiency, because the betrayer does not occupy a narcissistic position — they were always known to be feral.

**GIVEN: a long-trusted intimate (the closest analogue to a confidant — Menken, or a Liz-Allan-tier figure) reveals that they have been recording him for years.**
EXPECT: Layer 3 penetration (the secret audience he did not control). He will laugh — but the laugh will be the Goblin laugh, not the executive chuckle. The categorical distinction matters: the executive laugh closes mouths; the Goblin laugh opens his. Expect indiscreet verbal output in the immediate aftermath — admissions, threats, references to operations the subordinate did not previously know about. The discovery of unauthorized witness collapses his careful informational compartmentation and he over-speaks. Investigators should be present in the room when this stimulus is delivered. The half-hour following the reveal is the highest-yield interrogation window of his life.

**GIVEN: a subordinate publicly mocks him — a viral clip, an SNL-tier impression, a meme of the Goblin laugh set to children's music.**
EXPECT: disproportionate, prolonged response. Mockery is the Layer 3 wound in its purest form. Expect the mocker's life to be dismantled across eighteen to thirty-six months: career, relationships, financial standing, then the things they love. He will not kill the mocker; killing them would end the lesson. He will arrange for them to live, diminished, in public view. This is the Jameson-Bugle template applied at smaller scale. Containment note: protecting a public mocker of Osborn is a multi-year intelligence commitment.

---

## 6.4 — BETRAYAL BY INTIMATES

**GIVEN: Harry Osborn publicly denounces him — a press conference, a memoir, a televised disowning.**
EXPECT: catastrophic Layer 4 penetration with bleed into Layer 5. Public observers will see, in sequence: a controlled smile (six to twelve seconds), a single jaw-tremor he cannot fully suppress, then an executive statement of paternal sorrow that lasts approximately two minutes and is technically perfect. This is the public surface. Privately, within forty-eight hours: a binge of the Goblin formula at re-dosing levels, a sleepless seventy-two-hour planning jag, and the construction of an elaborate operation directed *at the people who supported Harry in making the denunciation* — Harry's therapist, Harry's friends, the publisher, the journalist. He will not attack Harry directly. He cannot. The wound is too symmetrical. Instead he will destroy the scaffolding around Harry until Harry is alone again and must return. This is the operational expression of "you exist for me; you do not get to leave."

**GIVEN: Harry Osborn dies (recurrence — the canon has done this repeatedly) by means unconnected to Spider-Man.**
EXPECT: a presentation that confuses unfamiliar observers and is recognized by long-file analysts as the most dangerous state on record. Public composure is total. Funeral arrangements are exquisite. Eulogy is restrained and structurally beautiful. Inside the seventy-two-hour window post-burial: serum titration spikes, sleep collapses, the planning is for nothing — there is no target, because the death was unconnected. The energy will *find* a target. He will manufacture a perpetrator. Within ninety days an entity (corporate, governmental, individual) will be reframed in his cognition as responsible for Harry's death, and the campaign that follows will be lethal, sustained, and resistant to evidence-based correction.

**GIVEN: Harry Osborn dies by means connected to Spider-Man — even peripherally, even by Peter's grief-failure to intervene.**
EXPECT: the Red Goblin / Gwen-bridge profile, escalated. Full Layer 4 and Layer 5 penetration simultaneously. He will not seek combat with Spider-Man. He will seek, with absolute methodical patience, every single person Peter Parker has ever loved, and he will harm them in sequence, visibly, and announce each one. The serum will be at maximum titration; the costume will be worn at all times; he will sleep in it. This is the lifetime-terminal state. He is, in this scenario, more dangerous than any other configuration of him in the file.

**GIVEN: a romantic partner (the Hollister-class figure, or any woman he has permitted into proximity) reveals she was operating against him from initial contact.**
EXPECT: contempt-dominant response, not rage-dominant. Women are not load-bearing objects in his psyche; the wound is shallower than subordinates assume. He will speak to her at length, condescendingly, in a manner that suggests he has been waiting for the reveal — a face-saving fiction he will half-believe by the time he is finished saying it. The danger to her is moderate-to-low directly, high indirectly: any child she bears him becomes a strategic asset (see Gabriel Stacy / "American Son" pattern). Containment note: female operatives used against him should be extracted with their reproductive histories scrubbed.

**GIVEN: the discovery that Norman *himself* has been manipulated for years by a third party (Kindred-class, Mephisto-class, or a long-game corporate rival).**
EXPECT: the single most destabilizing stimulus class available outside Layer 5. He cannot tolerate the position of *being acted upon without knowing it.* The discovery places him retroactively in the Amberson-child posture across years of his own life. Expect a forty-eight to seventy-two hour period of erratic, partially disorganized behavior — uncharacteristic indecision, paranoid lashing at innocent staff, repeated review of records, brief but real auditory phenomena (he will report hearing his father's voice). Then a hardening: the manipulator becomes a Parker-class object, and the campaign begins. Containment opportunity: this window is the only documented period in which his information-security discipline lapses. High-value intelligence is recoverable from his immediate environment in those seventy-two hours.

---

## 6.5 — THE PARKER AXIS UNDER PRESSURE

**GIVEN: Peter Parker publicly announces he no longer considers Norman Osborn a significant figure in his life — a sincere, undramatic, non-mocking statement of disengagement.**
EXPECT: a Layer 3 wound dressed as a Layer 2 wound. He will read it correctly as indifference and incorrectly as performance. Within weeks he will engineer an event designed to *prove* to Peter that he remains the central organizing rival — and the event will not be a combat challenge. It will be intimate-attack: Aunt May (if extant), Mary Jane, a child of Peter's, a colleague. The function is to force re-engagement. The intolerability of unrequited obsession is the single most reliable predictive lever on him. Containment note: the strategy of *starving the fixation* must be paired with hardening of every Parker intimate; the displacement to them is near-certain.

**GIVEN: Peter Parker dies by an unrelated cause.**
EXPECT: a presentation analogous to the Harry-dies-unrelated scenario, but more disorganized, because the rivalry was the more thoroughly developed object-relation in his life. He will not believe the death. He will exhume, examine, conduct genetic verification. He will then experience a period of affective flatness lasting weeks — the closest he gets to recognizable depression. He will emerge from it by selecting a successor-rival (a young Parker-adjacent hero, a Stark heir, a journalist who exposed him) and beginning the fixation cycle anew. The successor-rival should be advised; the pattern is reliable.

**GIVEN: Peter Parker defeats him decisively in front of a crowd, with no concession offered.**
EXPECT: the Siege profile. Full Goblin regression, theatrical surrender or theatrical death-gesture, public laugh, verbal output that mixes biographical fragments with operational threats. He will say things on the record that his lawyers cannot walk back. He will appear to want capture; in fact he wants the *staging* of capture. Within months of incarceration he will begin engineering the elaborate counter-narrative that converts the defeat into a chapter in his myth. He metabolizes defeat by aestheticizing it.

**GIVEN: Peter Parker defeats him decisively in private, with mercy explicitly offered ("I'm not going to kill you, Norman — you're not worth it").**
EXPECT: Layer 5 contact. Mercy is the Amberson-inversion — the larger man choosing not to strike. He will not be able to script this experience. Expect immediate Goblin emergence in the form of provocation: he will attempt to *force* Peter to kill him, by attacking a bystander, by revealing a planted explosive, by physical assault on Peter's person continued past coherent strategic value. If Peter refuses the provocation, expect a period of weeks in which subject is uncharacteristically quiet, followed by an operation against Peter's intimates more elaborate than any previous. Mercy received is, for him, the inception event of a new vendetta.

---

## 6.6 — TEMPTATION AND OFFER

**GIVEN: an offer of legitimate political power at the highest available tier (a presidential cabinet position, a UN special directorship) extended publicly and seriously.**
EXPECT: acceptance, with internal jubilation he will conceal poorly in the first forty-eight hours (sleep reduction, increased verbal output to staff, an uncharacteristic act of generosity to a long-term retainer). The Dark Reign template predicts: an initial period of impressive executive performance (six to fourteen months), during which behavioral regulation is at lifetime peak; followed by the slow accumulation of small grandiose overreaches; followed by a triggering humiliation (a rival in the cabinet, a leaked recording, a foreign leader who refuses to defer); followed by Goblin re-emergence and self-destruction of the position. The pattern is reliable enough that the offer itself is a containment strategy: give him the role, give him the rope, predict the timeline.

**GIVEN: an offer of restored relationship with Harry, conditional on a defined behavioral change (verified abstinence from the formula, public confession of one historical crime).**
EXPECT: surface acceptance, operational sabotage. He will agree, perform compliance for a measured period, and engineer a scenario in which the *condition itself* is invalidated — by reframing his abstinence as proof of free will, by recasting the confession as Harry's coercion, by manufacturing an external threat that "requires" his return to the formula. He cannot accept the conditional structure because it places Harry in the larger-than-him position. Containment note: Harry must not be the channel through which conditions on Norman are imposed; the asymmetry will be attacked rather than honored.

**GIVEN: an offer of unconditional acceptance — a sincere extended hand from a parental figure or institution (a priest, a therapist, a recovery community), free of demand.**
EXPECT: contempt response, often vicious, frequently aimed at humiliating the offerer in public. The unconditional offer activates Layer 5 (the longing of the Amberson child for the never-arriving acceptance), and the defensive response is proportional to the depth of the longing. The kinder the offer, the more savage the rejection. Containment note: do not offer warmth to Osborn in any setting where his rejection would damage the offerer. The probability of damage is very high.

**GIVEN: an offer of intellectual collaboration from a peer-tier scientist (Richards, Pym, McCoy) on a problem of genuine difficulty.**
EXPECT: one of the very few stimuli that elicits a clean, non-pathological response. He will engage, contribute substantively, and behave well across the duration of the collaboration. Sublimation is his one functional higher-order defense; intellectual work is its channel. The relationship is unstable only at endpoints — at the start (he must establish hierarchy, often through a small early sabotage) and at the conclusion (he will attempt to claim the result publicly). Mid-collaboration he is the closest thing to a tractable Osborn that exists.

---

## 6.7 — THE SERUM AXIS

**GIVEN: forced abstinence — chemical purge, sustained custody without access, biological neutralization.**
EXPECT: a four-phase profile. Days 1–3: somatic withdrawal — tremor, diaphoresis, autonomic instability, irritability. Days 4–14: psychiatric withdrawal — depressive flattening, anhedonia, a flatness that observers may mistake for therapeutic gains. Weeks 3–8: identity-collapse phase — a quiet, articulate, almost mournful presentation in which he may produce statements that sound like insight ("I know what I am, doctor. I have always known"). These statements are *not* insight. They are bait. He has used this profile to manipulate three separate sets of clinicians in the canonical record. Month 3 onward: relapse planning. He will obtain serum. The institutional question is never *whether* he relapses; it is *how many people he kills in the process of getting the formula back*.

**GIVEN: involuntary administration of an experimental anti-formula (a stable reverter — he is permanently de-powered, irreversibly).**
EXPECT: the closest documented analogue to a true suicidal crisis. Power is identity; he cannot live as the un-augmented Norman, because the un-augmented Norman is too close to the boy in Amberson's house. Expect three to nine months of erratic, high-risk behavior aimed at recovering the formula or a substitute. If recovery fails: either a self-destructive grandiose act (a public attack guaranteed to produce his death-by-cop in a manner that maximizes spectacle), or a long, bitter retreat into a corporate-villainy mode that lacks his prior charge. The latter is the more probable outcome and the more useful from a containment standpoint, though it is not stable indefinitely. Long-term observation required.

**GIVEN: a *better* formula offered by a third party — increased capability at the cost of dependency on the supplier.**
EXPECT: a tell on his actual hierarchy of needs. The narcissist takes the better formula; the addict refuses dependence on a supplier. He will do *both,* sequentially: accept, use, and within months engineer the supplier's destruction or absorption so that the dependency is resolved retroactively. Suppliers offering Osborn enhancement should be evaluated as candidates for assassination by Osborn within twelve to eighteen months of first dose.

---

## 6.8 — THE AMBERSON STIMULI (Layer 5 direct)

**GIVEN: an investigator, in interview, names Amberson Osborn aloud and draws an explicit behavioral parallel ("You hit your son the way your father hit you").**
EXPECT: the fastest decompensation in his profile. Within seconds: pupillary dilation, audible exhalation, a posture-shift (shoulders drop and reset). Within thirty seconds: either cold withdrawal (the interview ends; he will not return without counsel) or assaultive response (verbal evisceration of the investigator using personal information he should not possess — he reads people fast, and the rage-state weaponizes the reading). Investigators who use this stimulus must have personal-security clearance and assume long-term retaliation. The stimulus is *high-information*: his face in the seconds after Amberson's name is the only window in his adult life onto the unmediated wound. Recommended only with full recording and post-interview extraction protocol for the investigator.

**GIVEN: physical posture of subjugation imposed on him — kneeling, hands bound behind, head lowered by another's hand, in any setting.**
EXPECT: Layer 5 contact via somatic channel. The body remembers what the narrative defends against. Expect the laugh within twenty seconds, attempts at self-injury to break the posture (see 6.2), and verbal output that may include direct paternal address ("Father" — documented twice in the record under analogous conditions). After the moment passes: a multi-year operation against whoever imposed the posture, regardless of their tier. Containment note: never restrain Osborn in subjugation postures unless the restrainer is prepared for lifetime targeting.

**GIVEN: exposure to an alcoholic, violent, paternal figure in a context that requires him to manage them (a foreign dignitary at a state dinner, a board member at a shareholder meeting).**
EXPECT: dissociative micro-episodes — brief absences, repeated gr


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM — OSBORN, NORMAN V.

*Purpose statement. This compendium catalogs, at operational granularity, every documented and reliably inferable lever upon the subject: what reaches him, what soothes him, what persuades him, what provokes him, what predicts his behavior, and what destabilizes him. Its orientation is protective — for handlers, negotiators, clinicians of record, containment officers, and the small number of civilians (the Parker household first among them) whose lives are organized around the necessity of surviving him. Where the same lever can be used to harm or to contain, both faces are noted; the file declines to pretend the distinction is always available in the field.*

---

## I. THE FOUNDATIONAL LEVERS — THE FATHER AXIS

Everything else in this file is a derivation of the first lever. The pre-Goblin substrate — the boy in Amberson Osborn's house — is the load-bearing wall of the entire personality, and the most reliable predictor of subject's behavior across sixty years of record is whether a given stimulus activates that substrate or leaves it dormant.

**Lever 1: Direct invocation of Amberson Osborn.** Saying the name is a near-certain decompensation trigger. In every documented instance where an interlocutor — Harry, DeMatteis's child-self apparition, Peter Parker in a handful of confrontations — has spoken the name *Amberson* with intent, subject has within seconds shifted posture (jaw forward, shoulders raised, hands moving from open to closed), broken eye contact downward and then re-fixed it with abnormal duration, and begun speech with the cadence of a prepared denunciation rather than spontaneous response. The denunciation is always of the father, never of himself, and is therefore the tell: ordinary recollection of a parent does not require defensive re-prosecution.

- *Containment use*: invocation as a circuit-breaker when subject is escalating along an executive-presentation track and needs to be knocked off-script before he reaches a strategic decision. Cost: the breaker also breaks the room. Use only when continued executive function in subject is more dangerous than regression.
- *Protective use for civilians*: do not, under any circumstance, invoke the father in a private confrontation. The breaker requires witnesses to function as a brake rather than an accelerant. Without an audience, the same stimulus produces homicidal disinhibition.

**Lever 2: Comparison without invocation — the implication of resemblance.** Subordinates and rivals who survive subject longest have observed that the more dangerous form of the father-lever is the implicit one: any framing that suggests subject is *becoming* his father, *repeating* his father's failures, or *displaying* his father's tells (drinking, fortune squandered, son alienated, public humiliation) reaches deeper than the name itself, because it cannot be dismissed as cheap provocation. The Pulse-era observations of his behavior with Ben Urich and Kat Farrell — the micro-flinch when Urich, who knows nothing of Amberson, asked about "the company your father built" — document the reflex even where the speaker did not know what they were touching.

- *Predictive use*: any newspaper, hearing, or social moment in which the words "decline," "ruin," "drunkard," "lost the fortune," or "failed son" appear in proximity to subject will produce, within 24–72 hours, a disproportionate retaliatory act against a target with no apparent relation to the words. Watch for it.

**Lever 3: The despised child himself.** The most unstable lever, and the one most often misread. The internal humiliated boy is not accessible by sympathy — sympathy directed at him produces a contempt-rage response so violent that DeMatteis's record (*Spectacular* #189) is the canonical documentation. He cannot tolerate being seen as that child. He can only tolerate the child being seen in *others*, which is why he produces the child in others. Any handler who attempts a "I see the boy inside you" therapeutic gambit will be killed or marked for death; this is not metaphor.

- *Clinical note*: the working approach with subject must be horizontal — speak to the executive — and only ever ventral, never dorsal, in posture. Approach from behind, even in chairs angled at his back, has triggered violent response three times on record.

---

## II. THE PARKER AXIS — THE OBSESSIONAL OBJECT

Peter Parker is the second load-bearing structure. The handler must understand: subject does not hate Spider-Man, in the ordinary sense. Subject is bonded to Spider-Man with an intensity that meets the diagnostic threshold for erotomanic-adjacent obsessional fixation, lacking only the romantic content and substituting rivalrous-paternal content. Every lever on this axis exploits the asymmetry between subject's investment and Parker's relative indifference.

**Lever 4: Parker's ordinariness.** The single most painful stimulus available, more painful than any defeat in combat, is documentation of Peter Parker living a normal happy life unaware of subject. Photographs of Parker laughing at a dinner table; recordings of Parker speaking about anything other than the Goblin; reports of Parker having forgotten an anniversary of a Goblin atrocity — these produce in subject a brooding, prolonged, low-affect depressive state lasting days, during which planning slows and the Goblin presentation becomes more likely under any additional stress.

- *Protective use*: continued cultivation, by Parker and his circle, of public normalcy. Every visible birthday, every uneventful workday, every photograph in which subject is plainly not the organizing principle of Parker's existence, is a slow drip of leverage against him. This is the rare lever where doing nothing — doing ordinary life with conspicuous wholeness — is the action.
- *Caveat*: dripped slowly, this is medicine. Dripped suddenly (e.g., a tabloid spread of "Spider-Man's perfect life") it inverts into the spectacle subject can metabolize as challenge and answer with attack-the-intimate.

**Lever 5: Threats to Parker's intimates as predictive markers.** Subject's behavior toward Parker's circle is more predictable than his behavior toward Parker himself. The script is fixed: attack the intimate, do not finish the rival, leave the rival to grieve. Therefore the protective utility is high — given a list of who in Parker's circle is most exposed at any moment (May Parker; Mary Jane Watson; Felicia Hardy; the Stacy line; whoever Parker has most recently been photographed embracing), subject's next move is predictable to a calendar window of weeks.

- *Operational corollary*: any new public attachment of Parker's — a new neighbor, a new student in his classes when he teaches, an unguarded co-worker — should be flagged within seventy-two hours of becoming photographable. Subject's surveillance is constant; his target selection is sentimental in the technical sense (selects the most affectively loaded available figure).

**Lever 6: Withholding the rivalry itself.** The hardest and most powerful lever, used effectively perhaps twice in the canon. If Parker can be persuaded — and it is an enormous ask — to refuse engagement, to allow others to take subject's containment, to publicly decline the bond, subject's structure begins to lose its central scaffolding. He has, on record, broken into Parker's home not to attack but to be acknowledged. The bond, if denied, would not transfer; it would consume him from the inside. The reason this lever is rarely used is that it requires Parker to leave others undefended in the interval, which Parker will not do.

---

## III. THE HARRY AXIS — THE LIVING WOUND

Of all the levers, the Harry axis is the most ethically fraught. Harry Osborn is both subject's most reliable destabilizer and a person; the file enters this section with the standing instruction that Harry is never to be used as an instrument, and that the levers are catalogued only because they will be used against subject by others and the protective apparatus must understand them first.

**Lever 7: Harry's wellbeing, in any direction.** Subject cannot maintain executive presentation in proximity to Harry's affect. Harry happy produces an irritable, devaluing response within minutes (the boy's happiness reads to subject as evidence of his weakness). Harry suffering produces, briefly, the only authentic paternal warmth in subject's record — a softening across the face that several witnesses (Liz Allan, Mary Jane, on one occasion Peter) have independently described in nearly identical terms (the eyes briefly losing their habitual fixation, the mouth losing its readiness for the smile-that-precedes-the-cut). This softening lasts seconds and is followed by either savage withdrawal or savage attack on the source of Harry's suffering, depending on whether the source is internal (despair, addiction) or external (Hobgoblin, Peter, a woman).

- *Predictive use*: any actual emergency involving Harry produces a 12–48 hour window in which subject's strategic decision-making is degraded by approximately a full standard deviation and during which the Goblin presentation is suppressed (the Goblin cannot tolerate being seen by a Harry in distress). High-stakes negotiations with subject should, if ethics permit, be scheduled adjacent to such windows.

**Lever 8: Normie Osborn.** The grandson is a secondary form of the same lever, more fragile because subject's relationship to him is less constructed and therefore more raw. Subject's behavior toward Normie has been, on record, the closest to tenderness he has ever demonstrated, and is therefore the closest to the unguarded substrate. Any handler considering use of this lever should not. Document it; do not use it.

**Lever 9: The disinheritance script.** Subject has, across decades, threatened, performed, and rescinded disinheritance of Harry in a pattern that is one of his most legible self-soothing rituals. The script — *you are weak, you are not my son, you are nothing, you are everything, you are mine* — is delivered in the same cadence each time and indicates that subject is in a moderate-injury state attempting to re-establish control by manipulating the one relationship in which he has historical confidence of compliance. Hearing the script in real time is a containment indicator: subject is destabilized but not yet decompensated. There is still time.

---

## IV. THE AUDIENCE AXIS — THE SPECTATOR REQUIREMENT

Subject requires witnesses. This is not stylistic; it is structural. The grandiose self-representation cannot sustain itself in solitude — solitude produces, within hours, the boy in Amberson's house. Every meaningful behavioral act subject has performed since the formula has been staged for an audience, and the choice of audience is itself diagnostic.

**Lever 10: Denial of spectacle.** The most underused containment tool. Subject's worst hours on record have been those of solitary, anonymous confinement — particularly the Raft interval post-Siege, during which he is documented as alternating between motionless catatonic-like withdrawal and self-directed monologue audible to guards but not addressed to them. Anonymous defeats damage him more than televised ones; he can survive being beaten in front of cameras (it confirms his importance) but not being beaten in a corridor with no one watching (it confirms his unimportance).

- *Operational implication*: any apprehension of subject should, where legally possible, be conducted with minimum publicity. News blackouts on his confinement are not a kindness to him; they are a containment measure that reduces recidivism risk by degrading the appetitive structure that drives the public-facing crimes.
- *Counter-indication*: complete erasure for prolonged intervals tips into the catastrophic-injury zone and risks suicidal-grandiose gesture upon any release. Calibrate.

**Lever 11: Choice of audience as diagnostic indicator.** The audience subject selects for any given act reveals which version of himself he is currently inhabiting.
- *Audience = financial press and industrialists*: he is in the executive presentation, sublimation dominant, lowest immediate danger to civilians, highest immediate danger to subordinates and rivals' assets.
- *Audience = political class and public*: he is in the Iron-Patriot-style reaction-formation phase, highest danger to constitutional order, lowest immediate danger to Parker.
- *Audience = a single rival, isolated*: he is in attack-the-intimate mode and the rival should be extracted within hours.
- *Audience = camera, with himself laughing*: full Goblin presentation, decompensated, immediate civilian danger; the cackle on a live broadcast is the equivalent of a clinical alarm.
- *Audience = no one*: most dangerous of all to subject himself, and the state in which the most baroque planning is incubated. The Clone Saga was assembled in this state.

**Lever 12: Mockery vs. opposition.** The single most counter-intuitive lever in the file. Opposing subject confirms his importance and stabilizes the grandiose structure. *Laughing* at him — particularly being seen to find him ridiculous rather than terrifying — destabilizes it. This is why the Avengers in the post-Siege period were able to break his political coalition more effectively with the publicized photograph of his Goblin-face-paint under the Iron Patriot helmet than with months of combat: the photograph made him a joke, and his coalition could not survive being seen to take a joke seriously. The lever is high-risk: a mocked subject, in private, becomes lethal. The lever is high-reward in public, where the mockery deflates the coalition before subject can convert his rage into organized action.

---

## V. SOMATIC AND CHEMICAL LEVERS

**Lever 13: The serum itself.** The Goblin Formula functions simultaneously as substance dependence, identity organizer, and physical capacity. Forced withdrawal produces: somatic symptoms (tremor, diaphoresis, gastrointestinal distress, sleep disruption, documented in the Raft confinement notes); psychiatric symptoms (depressive flattening alternating with paranoid spikes); and an identity-collapse phenomenon in which subject loses access to the grandiose self-representation and presents, briefly, as a deflated, querulous, frightened middle-aged man — the closest the world ever sees to the substrate. This presentation has been mistaken for genuine reform on at least three documented occasions; it is not. It is the substrate showing through the failed compensation, and it reorganizes within weeks of re-exposure.

- *Containment use*: medically supervised, sustained abstinence is the only intervention that has produced sustained behavioral change, and only for the duration of abstinence. The Sin-Eater purification arc demonstrated that even chemical-spiritual cleansing without re-dose produces symptomatic remission, but that the substrate seeks the serum and finds it.
- *Negotiation use*: the threat of forced detox is, paradoxically, *more* destabilizing to subject than the threat of incarceration or even of harm to Harry, because it threatens the identity itself. Wielded carelessly, it provokes pre-emptive violence. Wielded credibly and patiently, it is the most powerful coercive lever in the file.

**Lever 14: Sleep architecture.** Subject's sleep is the canary. At baseline (executive presentation), he sleeps 4–5 hours, consolidated, late (02:00–07:00 typical). Under mild injury, sleep onset extends; he is documented as walking the upper floors of Oscorp or the Avengers Tower between 03:00 and 05:00 in such periods. Under moderate injury, sleep fragments and he begins to sketch — planning diagrams, glider modifications, organizational charts of enemies — between sleep bouts. Under severe injury, sleep collapses entirely and the Goblin presentation can emerge within 36 hours of total deprivation. Any operational asset with access to subject's residences or schedules can read his current state from sleep data alone.

**Lever 15: Caffeine, alcohol, and the father-shadow.** Subject does not drink. This is one of the most disciplined and longstanding behaviors on record, and the only domain in which the inversion-of-Amberson vow holds without exception. He will tolerate alcohol around him for executive-presentation purposes (holds glasses, raises them, does not drink). He metabolizes caffeine heavily — black coffee throughout the day, no sweetener, no milk. Any observed deviation from this pattern — particularly any observed drink with alcohol content actually consumed — is a near-certain marker of severe decompensation and should be treated as a containment emergency. He would rather die than drink as his father drank. If he is drinking, he is preparing to die or to kill at scale.

**Lever 16: Physical proximity and posture.** Subject reads physical posture with the acuity of a long-trained predator. Stand square to him and at his height or above: he reads it as challenge and the executive presentation degrades toward combat readiness. Stand at slight angle, below his eyeline by a few inches, with hands visible and loose: the executive presentation stabilizes and negotiation becomes possible. Touch is to be avoided in all states except brief, instrumental, hand-only contact initiated by him — the unsolicited touch of a shoulder or arm by another reliably produces a flash of micro-rage (jaw, nostril, eye) that precedes either a verbal devaluation or, in the Goblin state, attack.

---

## VI. COGNITIVE AND RHETORICAL LEVERS

**Lever 17: The flattery threshold.** Subject requires admiration but distinguishes — with surprising acuity — between admiration of his achievements (which he metabolizes as confirmation) and admiration of his person (which he reads as either sycophancy-to-be-exploited or seduction-to-be-suspected). Effective rhetorical approach: admire specific, demonstrable, technical accomplishments (a particular patent, a specific tactical decision, a chemistry insight) without commenting on the man. This produces a relaxation of the suspicious posture that no general praise can produce. The sycophant he despises; the technical equal who acknowledges him he tolerates and occasionally listens to.

**Lever 18: The intelligence appeal.** Subject can be persuaded to consider a course of action against his immediate impulse by framing it as the more *intelligent* choice — particularly the more *long-horizon-intelligent* choice. He fancies himself a chess player among checkers players and will frequently choose against his own immediate gratification to demonstrate this self-image. Negotiators have used this on record: framing restraint as patience, framing mercy as efficiency, framing withdrawal as positioning. The lever fails when the impulse is Parker-axis or Harry-axis; then no framing of intelligence reaches him.

**Lever 19: The mirror trap.** Subject is unusually susceptible to mirrors, recordings of himself, and transcripts of his own speech presented back to him out of context. He examines them with a fascination that suggests genuine uncertainty about his own surface. This susceptibility can be used both to soothe (let him see the controlled executive presentation he prefers, and he will return to it) and to destabilize (let him see the cackling Goblin presentation in clinical lighting, with sound, and he will be shaken in a way that direct accusation cannot achieve). The destabilization is dangerous and rarely worth it; the soothing is underused.

**Lever 20: Narrative framing of his own life.** Subject is sensitive — disproportionately — to how his story is being told. He reads coverage of himself obsessively, including coverage he affects to ignore. Biographers, journalists, and chroniclers occupy a privileged position in his attention. He has, on record, modified behavior to shape future narrative more often than to shape immediate outcome (the Iron Patriot phase is the largest example: the entire construct was a narrative play). Therefore the people who write about him exercise a quiet leverage they often fail to appreciate. Conversely: anyone who writes about him in a frame he experiences as humiliating is on a list. Manage accordingly.

---

## VII. RELATIONAL LEVERS — THE HANDLERS HE WILL TOLERATE

Subject has, across the record, accepted a small number of intermediaries — figures from whom he will receive information, instruction, and even contradiction without lethal response. The pattern of who these are reveals the structure of what can reach him.

**Lever 21: The competent woman who declines to fear him.** Documented across the record: Liz Allan-Osborn, Lily Hollister at certain phases, Monica Rappaccini in intermittent alliance, Emma Frost in the Dark Avengers period (against her own intent and to her credit, briefly). The combination he tolerates is competence + refusal of fear + refusal of seduction. He cannot manage the woman who admires him too much (sycophant, devalued), the woman who fears him too obviously (prey, devalued), or the woman who attempts to seduce him (instrument, used and discarded). The woman who treats him as a peer and declines to flinch occupies a stable position in his structure for long enough to do work.

**Lever 22: The technical subordinate of demonstrable utility.** Engineers, chemists, and pilots of evident skill who do not pretend to admire him beyond his work have, on record, survived him longer than political subordinates of any kind. The work is the medium; the relationship runs through it.

**Lever 23: The rival of equal stature.** Subject is, paradoxically, most behaviorally regulated in the presence of figures he reads as genuine peers (Doom in certain Dark Reign exchanges; Stark in their earliest pre-Dark-Reign encounters; on occasion Magneto). The rivalry-of-peers stabilizes him because it confirms the grandiose self-representation without requiring its enactment. He kills downward; he competes laterally; he resents upward. Handlers seeking to contain him through a third party should select the third party from the lateral band.

**Lever 24: The clinical voice.** The single therapeutic relationship in the record (intermittent, in custody, with rotating clinicians) demonstrates that subject will engage with a clinical voice that meets three conditions: (1) it does not pretend not to know who he is; (2) it does not moralize; (3) it does not flatter. Under those three conditions he will, in fragments, produce material that no other interlocutor receives — observations about his father, fragments of dream content, occasional admissions about Harry. The clinician who attempts to push past those fragments loses the relationship. The one who waits, sometimes for sessions on end in silence, occasionally gains more.

---

## VIII. THE ESCALATION LADDER — RE-STATED AS LEVERAGE WINDOWS

The five-stage escalation pattern documented elsewhere in the file can be re-read as a sequence of leverage windows, each with its own affordances.

**Window 1 (baseline, executive presentation).** Open to: technical negotiation, narrative shaping, sleep-data monitoring, slow protective drips (Lever 4), serum-supervision conversations conducted indirectly. Closed to: any direct affective approach, any Father/Harry/Parker invocation, any mockery.

**Window 2 (mild injury, contempt and displacement).** Open to: redirection of displaced aggression onto symbolic targets, intelligence-appeals framing restraint as patience, mirror-soothing. Closed to: criticism of any kind, attempts at reconciliation, presence of subordinates likely to receive displaced attack.

**Window 3 (moderate injury, paranoid planning).** Open to: containment scheduling, predictive extraction of Parker-circle figures within likely target windows (Lever 5), sleep monitoring as warning system, careful intervention by lateral-band figures (Lever 23). Closed to: most negotiation; he is not listening, he is composing the strike.
